Fu Bingchang's Lecture on Important Issues in the Book of Kinship and Inheritance (Continued) 58

In addition, the regulations on marriage age are also of great research value. Some advocate setting the age for men at twenty and for women at sixteen, but such vague advocacy cannot be considered an appropriate method. I have said that current legislation must not adopt arbitrary methods, but must be resolved scientifically. The actual situation in society should be studied. The existing laws of various countries still inevitably have arbitrary aspects, but they also take into account their current social situation. I remember that the Latin people near the Mediterranean, because they are close to the tropics, develop physically earlier, and the Catholic Church stipulates that the marriage

Page 9

Brief News 59

age should be fourteen for men and twelve for women. In central Europe, such as France and Belgium, people develop a little later, and they stipulate that the marriage age is eighteen for men and sixteen for women. In northern Europe, such as Norway and Sweden, the climate is cold and development is slower, and they stipulate that the marriage age is twenty-one for men and eighteen for women. Although the marriage ages set in these places are based on their local conditions and the relationship between the speed of people's physical development, they are still inevitably arbitrary. I stated earlier that I am raising the issue of marriage today for everyone to discuss. I personally have no absolute opinion. Just speaking of the marriage age, those who advocate late marriage believe that a low marriage age is very harmful to the economy and the race, especially in the economic aspect, because scientists believe that there is no major relationship in the racial aspect. However, the disadvantages of marrying too late are also numerous. For example, a man has fully developed by the age of fifteen, but legally he cannot marry until the age of twenty. What exactly is he like during these five years? We should not deceive ourselves when studying science. Can this man remain chaste until the age of twenty? I am afraid that although he has not formally married anyone, he has in fact already married someone. If he is forced to wait until a certain age to formally marry, he will definitely乱来 in fact. We have also studied this problem and believe that it cannot be solved. Various countries have tried to solve this problem and have written many theories, but they are all empty talk and have not been implemented, which shows that this problem is really not easy to solve. The points I have mentioned above are all what we should study, and it is extremely difficult to study them, because these problems are closely related to customs, habits, social economy, etc. In addition, there are many difficult problems that have been submitted by Dean Hu to the Central Political Conference for resolution, such as how to limit the marriage of relatives, as well as the property issues of husband and wife, the issue of concubines, the issue of the family, and the issues of inheritance, inheritance, and wills. How should these be regulated? These are the legislative principles of the two books of kinship and inheritance. We can only wait for the Political Conference to decide before we draft them accordingly. Some people also say, since the two books of kinship and inheritance are so important because they are related to customs, habits, and social economy, would it be good if we did not draft them temporarily? From the perspective of those of us who are responsible for drafting, there is nothing wrong with resting for a while. However, what is the reason for those who advocate not drafting them temporarily? They believe that the situation in China is changing very quickly, and there is no need to定一个永久的法律. For example, the issue of marriage is just 法子办的. Taking Shanghai and Guangzhou as examples, these types of problems have changed faster in recent years than in various countries. According to the statistics of the Shanghai court, more than fifty out of every hundred cases are divorces. This situation has already gone to the United States with the purpose of marriage being情欲. People in such places have almost no concept of succession and family, and they completely adopt the American concept of marriage. However, people in rural areas still want to maintain the concept of succession. They are墨守旧习 and do not change easily. This is the difference between cities and rural areas. If we take the changes in Shanghai as an example, I am afraid that it will走得快一些 than European countries, while the situation in rural areas will probably not be like Europe even after decades. If we legislate now and take the city as the standard, it will be too far away from the countryside. If we take the countryside as the standard, it will also seem inappropriate in the city, so it is better not to draft it temporarily and let local customs dominate. This view seems to have considerable reason on the surface, but at the same time, we must think about the fact that cases will not not occur just because we do not定法律. Since they occur, it is impossible to solve them all according to habit, and the law should be unified. Although we have not yet定出这个法来, unification is inevitable in fact, because this type of case is related to national policy, and the same case should not be solved differently. For example, when the Supreme Court翻理案件, if it encounters two cases of the same nature, it cannot have two different judgments just because one occurred in a city and one occurred in the countryside. Therefore, if we do not draft, we will always搁在不解决之中 these difficulties, and these problems are all related to principles. It is always more convenient for the Legislative Yuan to draft them, because comparatively speaking, it is of course more appropriate to solve this problem by legislative means than by interpreting the law. In short, of the above two statements, there is reason for advocating not drafting, and there is also reason for advocating drafting. Now we can only wait for the Political Conference to discuss and decide the principles before we follow them. (End)

▲Over a thousand bandits in the Zhejiang-Anhui border area of Guangde and Si'an were severely attacked by the Zhong and Hang Regiments sent by Zhejiang Province near Si'an a few days ago and suffered heavy losses. In Xinlinpu Town, more than ten bandit leaders, including Liang Laogong and Gu Laoxiao, were killed or captured alive. The remaining bandits fled in all directions. Now the people of Fanchang are at peace. The Wuhu Self-Defense Regiment, which was sent to assist in the suppression, set out and returned to Wuhu yesterday.

▲The city's Public Security Bureau arrested more than ten reactionary elements, including Peng Ziming, Yuan Limin, Pan Zefang, and Xu Baoting, in the Sanmei Nunnery the night before last upon provincial orders and seized many pieces of evidence. ▲This afternoon at 1 p.m., the Wuhu Municipal Government convened a joint meeting of the City Public Security Bureau Chief, County Magistrate, General Chamber of Commerce Chairman, City and County Party Committee members, and Finance Management Office Directors to discuss maintaining the people's livelihood. It was unanimously agreed that the rice reserves in Wuhu were less than 30,000 shi. Once the source of supply becomes scarce, not only will prices continue to rise, but there is also a danger of running out of food. It was decided that the rice gangs would raise funds to purchase 10,000 shi of foreign rice in preparation for famine relief at平价. As for the平糶 method, it was decided to convene rice businesses from Guangchao, Yanning, Longfang, and factories this Thursday to discuss how many shi can be proposed daily from the rice reserves for平糶 use, so as to start糶 on the same day to relieve the poor. It is planned to divide the平糶处 into five locations. The loss of rice prices will be compensated for in the future under the rice donation item.

▲The Wuhu Municipal Government demolished the city wall of Wuhu and built a ring road. Due to funding issues, only a part of the west city was demolished before the project was suspended. It has now been decided to bid for the sale of all the city bricks in sections, with each 10,000 bricks priced at 400 yuan. This price will be used for leveling the ground for the ring road and continuing to demolish the North Gate city tower to facilitate pedestrians.

▲Yesterday, two boatmen, Jiang Laowu and Xiao Zhang, who carried passengers from Wanzhi to Anhui, were robbed by bandits while traveling through Jingshan Lake, 20 li from Wuhu. Songjiang 61

The Anti-Smuggling Brigade Rescues Hostages The Fourth Brigade of the Su-Shu Anti-Smuggling stationed in Punan Shanyang suddenly heard intense gunfire in the northwest on the evening of the 19th. They immediately dispatched officers to be on the lookout. It was reported that more than ten bandit ships of the 太保阿书 gang were engaged in fierce battle with the troops led by Water Police Captain He Yalin in Jiaoli Bay. Pan Meiting, the head of the anti-smuggling brigade, immediately led his troops to join the county police team to assist in the battle. The bandits were already in retreat after being fiercely attacked by the water police. Blockades were set up in Jinshan mouth, Mapeng and other places. Two bandit ships were shot down, and the bandits landed and scattered. Two Mauser rifles were captured. On the following day, Qi Shouguang, patrol leader of the Fifth Anti-Smuggling Squadron, and others captured a bandit ship near Xihutang and rescued six hostages, Xu Asheng, Gu Yunchuan, Lu Longshan, Xu Runqing, Yang Qingshan, and Yang Zhujun, and one nine-ring rifle. Captain Pan interrogated and the hostages confessed that they were traveling to Shanghai on a Ningbo-Zhejiang liner when they were kidnapped by bandits. Their clothes were stripped, and they were in a very haggard state. Captain Pan has notified the families of the hostages to come to Shanyang to identify them, and he has also notified the county government for the record and reported to the Anti-Smuggling Bureau.

The County Prepares for Spring Sports The county-run middle school is now temporarily holding the first annual spring sports meet of the entire school at the public stadium on the 26th and 27th of this month, in accordance with the newly promulgated curriculum standards. Students are required to participate in at least one track and field event. The school has organized a sports committee to prepare, and County Magistrate Ni and Education Bureau Director Jin have been appointed as honorary presidents.

Suzhou 62

County Finance Bureau Borrows Money from Chamber of Commerce Yuan Xiaogu, Director of the Finance Bureau of Wu County, stated that the county's finances have recently been extremely depleted and that 88,000 yuan urgently needs to be allocated for prison expenses. He has raised funds from the Chamber of Commerce, with a term of six months and a monthly interest rate of 1.2%. The income from the busy season of the 19th year will be used to repay the loan. The Finance Bureau has also notified the Tianye Association to send representatives to attend the meeting at that time to discuss the matter together.

The Li-Cheng Mutual Lawsuit Case Concludes The case of the former State Councilor Li Genyuan, residing in Suzhou, and his concubine Cheng Peiyi mutually suing each other, has been repeatedly heard in court by the Wu County Local Court, and the case has not been concluded. The day before yesterday (21st), both parties were summoned to court again, and Judge Qin heard the case. The defendant, Monk Shi Ruhe, was also summoned to court. Li Genyuan also personally appeared in court, and lawyers Tang Shenfang and Zhu Fucheng debated. The hearing was adjourned, and the verdict is scheduled to be announced on the 28th of this month.

Chongming Local Bully Lu Yuren Tried Yesterday Lu Yuren, a local bully of Xiasha, Chongming County, was reported by someone and summoned by the Nanjing Special Court. Lu was formerly the county magistrate and caused deaths. After the trial, he was sentenced to death. Later, the case was transferred to the Jiangning Local Court for retrial. The original verdict was revoked, and the local bully was sentenced to four years of imprisonment. Lu refused to accept the verdict and appealed to the High Court and was held in the Third Sub-Prison of Siqian Street. Lu has a smoking habit. A few days ago, Zhuang Yan, the former magistrate of Changshu County, brought opium to visit Lu Yuren in prison and was discovered by the guards. Zhuang Yan was detained, and Director Lin of the High Court was asked to issue an order to transfer Zhuang to the Local Court for investigation. At the same time, Lu Yuren's visits were suspended. The opium delivery case will be jointly investigated and handled by the Local Court. The case of Lu's appeal as a local bully was investigated in court yesterday (22nd).

Wuxi 63

Petition to the Xichang Circuit to Postpone Construction Levy: The Xichang Provincial Road officially began its levy construction on the 18th. Yesterday, the township chiefs of the 10th District along the route repeatedly received requests from the public, stating that the commencement of construction coincided with the period of wheat ears, bean pods, mulberry growth, and silkworm activity in the countryside, and requested postponement of construction. A meeting was convened and it was decided to submit a report to the Provincial Government's Construction Department and the County Government, requesting that the commencement date be postponed until winter. Qian Huizhou, Zhi Hang, Guo Yaofen, and Hua Zanmei were elected as representatives to petition the province. Furthermore, the people in the Shouzizhi Township area believed that the Xichang Road was using a new line, requiring too much farmland and causing too great a sacrifice, and that the old line was simpler. Yesterday, they also appointed representatives to petition the provincial government.

May Revolution Commemoration Preparatory Committee: Yesterday afternoon, the Propaganda Department of the County Party Consolidation Committee convened representatives from various agencies and groups at the committee's auditorium to hold a preparatory meeting for the May Revolution commemoration. After discussion, six commemoration measures were decided upon.

Deputy Township Head Falsely Accuses Gambling: Sheng Jin Yu, the deputy township head of Huishan Township in our county, and Li Huanting, the lane chief, have long abused their power and exploited the villagers. Unexpectedly, the other day, they falsely accused Li Renquan, Li Shengshi, and other villagers of gathering to gamble at home and profiting from it, requesting their arrest from the First Branch of the Ninth Branch Bureau of Qianqiao Public Security. The branch sent police to investigate and arrest them, but found no gambling activity in the Li family. They had no choice but to take Li Renquan and Li Shengshi to the bureau for questioning. Director Lu suspected that there might be other circumstances involved and summoned the plaintiffs, Sheng Jinyu et al., to the bureau, and together with the defendants, sent them to the Public Security Bureau for investigation.

The Guo Zizhen Case Yields Another Criminal: Guo Zizhen, a villager of Bashiqiao Township in the Sixth District (Tianxiashi), was beaten to death in 1928. Subsequently, his son, Guo Baixuan, petitioned the county government, which forwarded it to the provincial government, and the county offered a reward for the arrest of the murderers, Zhang Yuhui, Dai Shoubao, Lu Jinhe, and Dai Apan. The other day, Guo Baixuan learned that the murderer Dai Shoubao had returned from Shanghai to Wuxi and was hiding at his home in Bashiqiao. He immediately went and arrested Dai and sent him to the Twelfth Branch Bureau of Public Security, which transferred him to the Public Security Bureau for investigation. Dai Shoubao's confession was cunning and evasive, denying any involvement in the beating death of Guo Zizhen. Qian Jun verified the confession and sent him to the county government for investigation.

Resolutions of the County Political Meeting: Yesterday, County Magistrate Sun convened the directors of the four bureaus of Public Security, Finance, Construction, and Education for the 38th county political meeting. The following resolutions were made: (1) Regarding the order to strictly ban diviners and astrologers, it was resolved that (A) the Public Security Bureau should conduct registration on a regular basis and encourage them to change to other occupations, (B) all out-of-town diviners and astrologers should be banned, and (C) a letter should be sent to the County Party Headquarters and the Education Bureau and Public Security Bureau of each district to earnestly persuade the people to break with superstition. (2) Regarding the provincial government's instructions to cancel the inspection of rice and grain passing through the border checkpoints from April 1st, and the previous order prohibiting rice and glutinous rice from leaving the province, it was resolved to submit a report to the provincial government for approval on how to handle the inspection of rice and grain in the future. (3) Regarding the fact that the land survey books for the land requisitioned for the Xicheng Road have not yet been submitted and repeated requests have not been answered, it was resolved to require them to submit replies separately within one week. If they delay again, the district books will be recalled and disciplinary action will be proposed.

(2) The County Government should conduct a thorough inspection of the work of the district chiefs in each district, and those with outstanding achievements should be commended, while those who are incompetent should be replaced immediately. (7) Regarding the case of police officers from the Fourth Branch of Public Security being shot and killed by the Guo Tangqiao security corps, it was decided that the County Government should instruct the district chief of the Fourth District to provide preferential compensation in advance.

Zhenjiang 65

Construction Plan of the Jiangsu Construction Department: Since Sun Hongji, the Director of the Jiangsu Provincial Construction Department, took office, a month has passed. The following is a summary of Sun's recently announced outline of the Jiangsu Provincial Construction Plan: (1) Road Construction: The total length of provincial and county roads that have been decided upon is 14,000 li. According to regulations, residents within five li of the roads have the obligation to build the roads. All roads should be straightened, and bridges and culverts are planned to be completed this year. (2) Water Conservancy: It has been found that in the Jiangbei area, various river routes have lost their effectiveness and benefits. It is now planned to hire German water conservancy experts to guide the Huai River plan, diverting three-tenths of the Huai River into the Yangtze River and seven-tenths into the sea. However, due to limited funds, only small-scale repair work can be done first. (3) Provincial Capital Construction: The Provincial Capital Construction Committee has been changed to the Construction Engineering Office. Previously, the bidding for the construction of the main roads of the provincial capital had yielded results. However, asphalt roads can be implemented later because the new main roads are not very firm at the base, and asphalt is prone to cracking, and it is also not commensurate with the overall construction. This item can save 18,000 yuan. As for the drainage ditch problem, the original plan was to use Guanhe River as the tailwater. After review, it was determined that using Guanhe River to discharge sewage would be detrimental to hygiene, and it is still planned to use the original old ditch.

Suzhou Education Community Comes to the Province to Petition: After the Suzhou Municipal Government was cancelled in principle by the Provincial Government meeting, tax revenue has sharply decreased, and various facilities have also been suspended invisibly. The education funds of the city have been in arrears for more than three months. Although the municipal schools have repeatedly urged the municipal government to issue the funds, they have ultimately been told to close down. Now they are about to fall into a state of starvation. The city's Education Association and Principals' Association have appointed representatives Zhang Jianchu, Jiang Xilan, Li Younong, and Gao Jianzhi to come to the province to petition the Provincial Government and the Education Department, and to take the opportunity to visit various primary schools and educational institutions.

Internal Personnel Appointed by the Construction Department: Since Sun Hongji took office as the Director of the Jiangsu Construction Department, he has been reluctant to make many changes to the staff of the department, so he has been slow to announce them. It was not until yesterday that he formally appointed them. Except for those who resigned on their own, the list of appointed officials is as follows: Chief Secretary Zhang Zhu (former Secretary-General of the Hangzhou Special Municipal Government), Secretaries Liu Baohe and Xia Chengdong, Chief of the First Section Kang Shizhen, Chief of the Second Section Wu Tongju, Chief of the Third Section Yu Qitai, Chief of the Fourth Section Sun Liang, Chief of the Fifth Section Hua Chengyun.

Qingjiang 68

Bank of China Pursues Debt from Huaiyin and Siyang Counties: Wang Xiaoxiang, the manager of the Bank of China in this area, filed a lawsuit against the governments of Huaiyin and Siyang counties for failing to repay the road loan. The Jiangsu High Court has now instructed the Huai'an County Government to take jurisdiction over the case. Accordingly, the county government yesterday sent a copy of the complaint to the governments of the two counties, instructing their respective finance bureaus to provide written replies. The original text of Wang's complaint is recorded as follows: "For protracted non-repayment, a copy of the printed evidence is submitted, requesting summons for trial and legal judgment, setting a time limit for completion, and bearing litigation costs. In November 1926, Huaiyin and Siyang counties acknowledged the share capital of the Jiangbei Long-Distance Bus Company and borrowed 12,768 yuan from our bank to purchase the second batch of cars for the Jiangbei Road Construction Bureau. The loan was secured by the special automobile tax collected by Huaiyin and Siyang counties, with each county bearing 6,384 yuan. The magistrates of Huaiyin County, Xu Tong, and Siyang County, Luo Lu, prepared loan receipts, which were sent to our bank for verification, with the expectation of full repayment of principal and interest by the end of December 1926. Our bank then allocated the funds accordingly, obtaining receipts. The loan was purely for the purpose of purchasing cars to increase the Jiangbei Long-Distance Bus Company's share capital, and our bank temporarily accommodated the situation with a letter of consent from the Jiangbei Road Construction Bureau and loan receipts from the governments of Huaiyin and Siyang counties. The loan was secured by the special automobile tax collected, and it should have been repaid early both legally and factually. However, the governments of Huaiyin and Siyang counties initially claimed that the funds had not been fully collected, and later used military supplies as an excuse, stating that the funds had been diverted for other purposes. Repeated demands have been ineffective. Now, the governments of Huaiyin and Siyang counties are being sued according to law. However, all special automobile taxes collected by Huaiyin and Siyang counties have been transferred to the Huaiyin and Siyang County Finance Bureaus for collection, and all remaining special automobile taxes are in the two county Finance Bureaus. It has been requested in writing that they be fully responsible and not spend them arbitrarily. Therefore, a copy of the official letter from the Jiangbei Road Construction Bureau and the receipts from Huaiyin and Siyang counties are submitted to be presented in court during the hearing. The noble government is requested to examine the case, summon the county magistrates and finance bureau directors of Huaiyin and Siyang counties to court, and order them to each pay 6,384 yuan and bear the costs of this trial. For all proceedings in this case, Zhong Qi, the bank's permanent legal counsel, is appointed to present the case in court."

Nantong 73

Nine-County Bandit Suppression Conference Held in Nantong: Li Changjiang, the commander of bandit suppression for the nine counties of Jiangbei, Nantong, Chongming, Haimen, and others, summoned the county magistrates and police captains of the nine counties to Nantong on the 21st to hold a bandit suppression conference at the Nantong Club. (2) Small, scattered bandits in each county will be the responsibility of the county police and security forces to suppress. (5) The nine-county bandit suppression command headquarters will be located at the Jiangshan Gate in Nantong. (6) An office will be established in Rugao.

Residents of Jianqiao Street Request Postponement of Demolition: The Jiaxing County Government's Construction Bureau decided to widen the street and rebuild the road from Jianqiao Street to West County Bridge. Buildings on both sides that obstruct the road line must be demolished by the 20th of this month. The deadline has passed, but due to various obstacles, the demolition has not yet been carried out. It is heard that the authorities have decided to enforce the demolition. More than 100 residents in the area have sent a letter to the Tianxing Liuhong Committee, which has jurisdiction over the area, requesting that the demolition be temporarily postponed to alleviate the people's hardship, as they have no suitable place to move to and are financially unable to relocate. However, the county government has already put this project out to bid and scheduled the start of construction, and cannot hinder the progress due to the relocation problem of the residents. They have been instructed to demolish the buildings in accordance with the regulations as soon as possible.

Jiashan 76

Fengjing Captures a Large Number of Bandits: The Fengjing Public Security Bureau learned that a large number of bandits were gathered in the countryside about three li outside of Xilan. On the afternoon of the 20th, they joined forces with the security regiment of the Second Company of the Garrison Brigade stationed in the town and other forces to surround and suppress the area, capturing more than 50 bandits, three guns, three hostages, and other evidence, and brought them all to Fengjing for temporary detention. After a brief interrogation, the brigade escorted the bandits to the Songhu Garrison Command for investigation. As for the three hostages, they were asked to come forward to claim them.

Security Corps Captures and Escorts Bandit Criminals: On the afternoon of the 20th, the Yaozhuangqiao Yaoxi Village Security Corps, together with the local public security police station, searched for bandits in the Wang Tianhan area of Yaodong Village, capturing Li Rong's aunt and her son-in-law Li Renfu, as well as Cai Along and three others. They found a photo of Yang Mei, the daughter of the Doufu shop owner who had been kidnapped by the bandit leader Xu Tianxiong in the town, and more than 100 other pieces of evidence, and escorted them all to the county public security bureau for investigation.

Tianning Temple Fair Causes Trouble: At Tianning Duixuegang, the temple fair was held the day before yesterday, with more than 100 dramas being performed and paraded. The team performing the story of "Killing Son to Avenge" (Wang's Mother) and the team performing "Iron Rooster" with more than 100 people quarreled over who should go first. The quarrel escalated into a fight, and the person performing "Killing Son to Avenge" wielded a kitchen knife and injured more than ten members of the "Iron Rooster" team in the head. One of them was in critical condition and was sent to Nanhui Hospital for treatment. The person performing "Killing Son to Avenge" saw the serious consequences of his actions and was unable to escape. He was chased and captured by the "Iron Rooster" team and subjected to private punishment.

Pinghu 77

Joint Jiangsu-Zhejiang Suppression of Eastern Countryside Bandits: The Eastern Countryside bandit Tai Bao A Shu has been rampaging through the Jiangsu-Zhejiang border area, robbing property and kidnapping people, causing harm to the villages. In order to eliminate the bandit scourge, the Jinshan County Government decided to send a large number of more than 400 military police on the early morning of yesterday to join forces with the troops stationed in this county to surround and suppress the Liujia Yankiao Bridge area. A special envoy was sent in advance with a secret letter to Ping Visited County Magistrate Fang and said that the bandits are now scattered in the Liujia Yankiao Bridge area, the six shops of the bridge, and the Wanchun Bridge area. Please be allowed to send troops and police to join in the suppression at the appropriate time in order to annihilate them in one fell swoop. County Magistrate Fang approved the request and consulted with the troops stationed in the city and dispatched a portion of the patrol team, which was loaded onto the Jiufeng Steamer yesterday morning and transported to Xin, followed by the troops stationed there, who were dispatched to Quan Gongting Yaqian and other places one after another to block the area in order to have the opportunity to join in the suppression. It was also learned that Battalion Commander Zhao Xunshi had arrived in Ping from He yesterday and was transferred to XinCang to command the suppression. As of the time of this report, it was only known that the military and bandits had had one encounter, but no further news was available.

Shangyu 78

Famine Concerns in Shangyu's Grain Supply: Even in the most bountiful years, the entire county's statistics show a shortage of rice for two to three months each year. Last autumn's drought, floods, and insect plagues were frequent, and the winter was followed by months of rain and snow, causing particularly severe damage to the southeastern villages. Since the beginning of spring, cries of mourning have been heard everywhere. Although the Provincial Disaster Relief Association allocated funds for disaster relief and Mr. Qian Junren, a native of the county, raised 4,000 yuan from the Beiping Disaster Relief Association to purchase corn and distribute it to various districts according to a set ratio, the small amount of aid was insufficient, like a drop in the bucket. Moreover, it was limited to extremely poor families, while those in the middle and lower classes who relied on rice for food were seized with great panic. The early rice that has gone to market in Ningbo now starts at 15 yuan and 6 jiao, and the highest quality rice will reach 17 yuan, but even at that price, there is no rice available. Partly, this is because a small number of rice merchants are hoarding and speculating, and partly, it is because neighboring counties have also suffered natural disasters and cannot afford to help themselves. It has been rumored recently that the granaries in the cities and villages will be opened, but this will only benefit farmers of a certain social standing, and the truly poor tenant farmers will receive little benefit. The Grain Consumption Committee, which was originally organized by the county government and enthusiastic local gentry, has not yet received the rice that the common people have been anxiously awaiting. Therefore, in recent days, the sounds of couples quarreling and children crying from hunger have filled the streets and alleys.

Conference Proceedings 83

The Fifth National Education Association Conference was held yesterday morning at nine o'clock, chaired by Vice-Speaker Jin Zengcheng. After the formalities, he said that the association was very honored to have Mr. Hu Zhantang give a speech today, and the audience applauded. Mr. Hu rose to speak as follows:

Hu Hanmin's Speech 84

▲ Politics and Education Cannot Be Separated

▲ Shortcomings of Dewey's Theory

▲ Strict Educational Advocacy

▲ Attention to Secondary Education System

Chairman and fellow comrades, I very much wanted to come and observe this National Education Conference earlier, but it happened that the central government had important matters to discuss, and I was unable to split myself, so I was unable to participate in the conference and the various group review meetings, which is very regrettable. This National Education Conference is more systematic than previous conferences, and the representatives from various provinces are also more complete. Education bureau chiefs from various provinces, counties, and cities have also participated, all of which are advantages of this conference.

The Ministry of Education, after years of research and discussion, has formulated this entire plan based on the educational purpose of the Republic of China as determined by the central government. I have only read it once and feel that it is generally very good. You are all education experts and will definitely be able to make better revisions to the original plan.

Your conference wanted me to say a few words, and now I will just report on my recent thoughts. There may be some dogmatic points, please give me your guidance.

The meaning of the two words "education" needs to be broad. Just in terms of nouns, China only had "teaching" in the past. The connection of the two words "education" can be found in Mencius. In essence, humans are always in life, and therefore always in education. The scope is very broad, just as the general understanding of the two words "politics" is that politics is the business of the masses, and governance is the governance of the masses. Humans are always in politics, and the scope is the same.

I often hear people say the phrase "separation of politics and education." The source of this phrase

was determined against religious autocracy. At the time when religious autocracy oppressed politics, politics was too restricted, and the call for the separation of politics and religion arose. It was introduced into China, also saying the separation of politics and religion. This was during the warlord and autocratic period, when it was ravaged and oppressed by force, seeking to separate from politics, and when it was not possible, it was still possible to say. As for now, in principle and in fact, it is not possible to say. Therefore, the two cannot be in the same space, and cannot exclude one and keep the other. Looking at various countries, they all promote the separation of politics and education, but in reality, education is not only not opposed to politics, but is appropriately complementary, and each forms its own independent academic style. This is because what politics and education require is actually the same. Its political purpose in China is nothing more than national independence, universal civil rights, and development of people's livelihood. Education is also nothing more than this.

The purpose of this Education Conference is to determine the direction of education, to wash away the old habits of educational waste and following conventions, and to focus on the implementation of the plan. Not only can politics and education not be separated, but there is also a close relationship everywhere. If politics is separated from education, then politics will not become politics, and if education is separated from politics, then education will not become education. During the period of political tutelage, various construction projects often feel the lack of academic development and the lack of talent training, which is clear evidence that politics cannot be separated from education. The Republic of China was founded without going through a period of political tutelage. Sovereignty rests with the people, but the people have no knowledge. Legislators are bought by others, and the people see it as unrelated. The so-called political tutelage, in literal terms, tutelage is education. The training of the four powers and what is emphasized during the period of political tutelage is also the matter of education. The importance of politics not being separated from education is like this.

Furthermore, when it comes to education, education cannot be completed if it is separated from politics.

The so-called ideal new village, Minister Jiang has said that this educational policy must be promoted with political stability and sufficient funding, which also shows that education cannot be separated from politics and stand alone.

In recent years, I feel that there is a major shortcoming in education, that is, the shortcomings of foreigners are often imported to the Chinese people. For example, Dewey comes, and his pragmatic education, the development of child-centered education, spread to China. Students compete for freedom and advocate the abolition of exams, and waves of trends arise, which is very regrettable. China's past education of simplicity and punishment was certainly inappropriate, but since Dewey's theory was imported into China, it has inevitably gone too far. Students are accustomed to romance, and even have slogans such as "Down with teachers who don't ask for leave." Education speculates and deceives young people, caters to their preferences, and uses the overthrow of patriarchal feudalism and capitalism as a talisman for its speculation. As a result, the academic atmosphere has been ruined beyond repair. Therefore, education must be stricter, and whether students should have discipline should be regarded as our reasonable demand, so that young people can deeply understand the necessity of maintaining discipline, that is, maintaining discipline is the obligation of the masses to society.

We should not be afraid of people's attacks on educational policies, such as advocating strict education, which will inevitably be commented on by advocates of liberalism and education like Dewey. However, our observation of Western educational theories, whether it is Dewey or Spencer, is just too much about freedom and too much about anarchism. For the current society and the current established Chinese society, I am afraid it will not work, and we have to oppose it. That is, if we expand and enrich Dewey's child-centered educational theory, then the Minister of Education must listen to the orders of the Director of Education, the Director of Education should listen to the orders of the school principal, and the principal and faculty should listen to the orders of the students. If the students unanimously direct the faculty to break in, the Ministry of Education can break into the Ministry of Education. How can it still be organized?

Most secondary schools in various countries advocate strictness. Graduates of secondary schools have been able to complete their civic personality. University graduates often specialize in one teacher and one profession, and the increase in knowledge is particularly large at this time. It is like the legacy of ancient China's setting up tents to teach. As for our country's university graduates, the relationship between teachers and students is very superficial as soon as they leave school, which is a pity.

We should regard education as a sacred cause. In politics, if we regard education as insignificant, educational funding is not valued, or we hold the view of teaching after becoming rich, thinking that educational expenses can be paid slowly, it is very inappropriate. China has vast land and abundant resources, so the reason why it is not rich is due to the lack of education. If we wait until we are rich before teaching, then the country will perish, so what is the use?

Those engaged in education should also regard education as the most sacred cause, and should be prepared to face all kinds of difficulties, even sacrifices. Before the European War, the salaries of university professors were less than those of a laborer, but educators deeply recognized that education is for education's sake, and the material rewards are far less important than the spiritual rewards. In short, in politics, we should find ways to protect education. In education, we should look at it from the perspective of the educated and bring it into the right track, and then there is hope of success.

China's poor secondary schools are the fatal wound of Chinese education. Is it the failure of the three-three system? At the beginning of the rise of the three-three system, one side thought of raising the level of secondary schools, and one side wanted to connect with universities. The original intention was very good, but in practice, neither side was able to do it. The current vocational subjects in senior high schools are not as good as the previous Class A vocational schools. Most families with children hope that their children can find employment after graduating from secondary school because they cannot afford the cost of university education. High schools, middle schools, and elementary schools should have requirements for connection, but at the same time, they should also consider those who do not connect in the principle of connection, and enrich the curriculum plan of senior high schools. We should pay special attention to this.

The above is just a miscellaneous talk based on my feelings, for your reference, and I hope you will give me your corrections.

Chairman's Response 85

Chairman Jin Zengcheng replied, saying that Mr. Hu Zhantang has given us instructions with his personal feelings and enthusiasm. I would like to thank Mr. Hu on behalf of the entire body.

Higher Education Group Report 86

▲ Huang Jianzhong reports on the results of the review

Next, Huang Jianzhong, Chairman of the Higher Education Group, reported on the results of the review and stated that the number of people at the meeting of the Higher Education Review Group was 22 for the first time and 16 for the last time. A total of five review meetings were held. As for the review results, they are described as follows:

(1) Revision of Term and Budget (Page 15 of the Original Plan)

1. Enrich the content of national universities. "Increase funding by 500,000 yuan per year" is changed to "Increase funding by 1 million yuan per year" plus "Subsidize private universities and specialized schools with 300,000 yuan per year."

2. Increase the number of students sent abroad. "Starting from the seventh year" is changed to "Starting from the 19th year." Funding "500,000 yuan" is changed to "300,000 yuan."

3. Prepare to establish specialized schools. "Starting from the fourteenth year" is changed to "Starting from the nineteenth year." "Increase funding by 1 million yuan per year" is changed to 300,000 yuan in the first year, and then increase by 200,000 yuan per year until it reaches 1.5 million yuan.

4. Reward academic research funds of 6 million yuan "to be paid in twenty years" is changed to "to be allocated in ten years," with an annual average of "300,000 yuan" changed to "600,000 yuan."

(2) Revision of Programs

1. The title of the first section is changed to "1. Measures to Enrich the Content of National Universities" (Page 1)

2. The "6th" in the first section is changed to "1st," and the following are deleted and changed to another section, the title of which is "2. Measures to Consolidate Existing Provincial Universities and Stipulate the Location for Establishing New Universities" (Page 5)

3. "11th" to "12th" in the first section are deleted and changed to "1st" and "2nd," and the "Reward Measures" are moved forward to form another section, the title of which is "3. Measures to Consolidate Private Universities and Specialized Schools" (Pages 6 to 7)

4. The numbers of sections 2, 3, 4, 5, 6, and 7 are changed in order to 4, 5, 6, 7, 8, and 9. However, the title of section 4 should be changed to "6. Measures to Increase the Number of Students Sent Abroad" (Pages 7 to 5)

Revision of the introduction: The following three words "this plan is exhausted" are proposed to be revised as follows: "It is proposed to use all efforts within the six-year period of political tutelage to enrich and improve the current content of universities, but to make qualitative improvements and not to expand in quantity. We will also try to increase the number of students sent abroad and prepare to establish specialized schools, and use the remaining resources to allocate funds for academic research in ten years" (Page 1)

Discussion on Higher Education 87

｜Resolution｜

▲ The deadline for funds is reserved according to the review report.

▲ National university professors should be full-time in principle. It is absolutely forbidden for full-time teachers at School A to be concurrently teachers or important staff at School B.

▲ The consolidation of private universities and specialized schools should still be carried out in accordance with the original plan.

▲ Other matters are passed according to the review report.

Zhu Jingnong said that the revision of the programs in this plan can be passed first, and the modification of the time limit and budget can be reserved for discussion after the budget group has reviewed it.

The chairman said, please start discussing the time limit.

Duanmu Kai said that the time limit is related to the funding, so the time limit and funding should be combined into one chapter and reserved, which was seconded by Lu Dianyang, but did not pass due to a minority.

Huang Jianzhong said that there is no need to reserve the time limit, which was seconded by Xie Shuying and Chen Bulei.

Zhu Jingnong said that the reservation of funding and the time limit have been discussed many times and can be voted on immediately. The chairman said that if there is no objection to the time limit, it will be passed.

Ou Yuanhuai said that the revision of the programs can be discussed first, which was seconded by Zhu Jingnong.

The chairman asked, is there any objection? If there is no objection, it will be passed.

Measures to Enrich the Content of National Universities 88

Liu Zhanen said that item C of the fourth point, "Improve teaching effectiveness," should be changed to "National universities should make great efforts to reduce staff and increase teachers, and be full-time in principle. The number of part-time teachers should not exceed one-third of the total number. It is absolutely forbidden for professors at School A to concurrently hold positions as professors or important positions at School B," which was seconded by Li Quanshi.

Xie Shuying said that university professors should focus on research, not on part-time teaching and part-time positions. The current trend of part-time teaching in domestic universities is enough to affect teaching effectiveness.

Zhu Jingnong said that he agrees with part-time teaching and part-time positions within a school, but opposes part-time teaching and part-time positions outside the school.

Shao Feizi said that the part-time teaching and part-time positions of teachers within a school should be strictly restricted. Zhao Naichuan said that professors and staff have the spirit of professors governing the school and should be promoted. Therefore, the four words "strictly restricted" should be changed to "discretionary measures." Wei Tingsheng said that if professors at School A are concurrently appointed as professors or important positions at School B, if it cannot be handled at their discretion, it will be difficult for those who have contributed to academic research, so he agrees to delete the four words.

Huang Jianzhong said that professors should be full-time in principle, and professors who hold part-time positions outside the school should be called lecturers. I think it should be changed to "Teachers in the same school who hold both administrative positions and staff who hold classes should be subject to discretionary restrictions."

Liao Maoru said that he agrees with Liu Zhanen's proposal, but the next paragraph should be changed to "It is absolutely forbidden for professors at School A to concurrently hold positions as professors or important positions at School B."

The chairman put it to a vote, and the proposal of those who supported Liu Zhanen was passed by a majority. Zhu Jingnong said that the next paragraph should be revised to say that it is absolutely forbidden for full-time teachers at School A to concurrently hold positions as teachers or important positions at School B, which was passed by a majority.

▲ Measures to Promote Education in Universities and Specialized Schools

Yu Qingtang proposed to retain the original plan.

Yang Xingfo said that the revision combines the original plan and does not mean to cancel the original plan.

Hu Shi Hua, please ask the chairman to put the revision to a vote.

The chairman put it to a vote, and the majority who supported maintaining the revision passed it.

▲ Measures to Improve the Level of Students in Universities and Specialized Schools and Seek Employment for Graduates

Liu Zhanen proposed that the tenth article of this measure should be added above "All universities in the country should have career guidance," and then followed by the original text, and the career visiting center should be changed to a career guidance center.

Zhao Naichuan said that career guidance is only necessary in secondary schools, and is not necessary in universities.

Huang Jianzhong said that it should be retained. Before the implementation of the examination, this method can still be applied. The chairman put the proposal of Ma Hetian to a vote, but it did not pass due to a minority. The chairman put the proposal of Liu Zhanen to a vote, but it did not pass due to a minority.

▲ Measures to Consolidate Private Universities and Specialized Schools

Wang Maozu proposed that this measure should add "All universities that have already been established should be strictly assessed by the Ministry of Education according to standards. Those that do not meet the standards should be rewritten as high schools, specialized schools, or other schools," which was seconded by Chen Bulei. Dai Qi said that there is no need to add this article, because item A of the crackdown measures already has this measure.

Education Funding Group Report 91

｜Review Results｜

(1) Revise various estimates

(2) Determine the source of funds

At 2 p.m. on the 22nd, the Education Funding Group held its second review meeting at the Ministry of Education. The committee members present were Zheng Hongnian, Wei Que, Huang Shiheng, Li Shi, Chen Dezheng, Hu , Zhang Honglie, Xu Shouzhi, Jiang Shaomo, Chen Hexian, Wei Tingsheng, and Wu Heling, a total of twelve people. Zheng Hongnian chaired the meeting and Chen Dezheng recorded it. In addition to revising the budget forms of each group separately, the Education Funding Review Report is recorded as follows:

The various education funds are all assumed numbers. For what can be called a budget, the Ministry of Education should be requested to determine the budget standard based on the facts after a certain number of years.

(A) Regarding the estimated number of each item,

(1) The revision of compulsory education funding is as shown in Table A. For the methods of provinces and cities undertaking compulsory education funding, see Item B. (2) The expenditure of adult supplementary education is as shown in Table B. Regarding the allocation of funds, a principle regulation should be set in the source clause. The percentage of the central government and local governments cannot be taken as a definite criterion and is omitted. (3) The funding of teacher training institutions has been included in the compulsory education funding and will not be listed separately. The fifth item of the Method for Establishing Teacher Training Institutions should be deleted, and the sixth item should be changed to the fifth item in Appendix 1. (4) Under the item of primary education, teachers Appendix 2. (5) The estimate of secondary education funding is as shown in Table C. (6) The estimate of higher education funding is as shown in Table D. (7) The estimate of social education funding, in addition to the expenses of establishing social education institutions in provinces, cities, and counties, is as shown in Table E. (8) The overseas Chinese education funding is as originally planned and set in Appendix 3. (9) The primary school and social education funding in Mongolia and Tibet are as set in the original plan, of which the amount borne by the central government should be as shown in Table E. (10) The general estimate table of the entire plan should be re-formulated by the Ministry of Education based on the above items 2 to 10.

(B) Regarding the source of education funding,

The source of education funding is determined as follows:

(A) Income used entirely for education funding (1) 50% of the revenue from Shatin official fees goes to the central government, 30% to the provinces, and 20% to the counties and cities (30% for special cities, and the rest goes to the central government) for allocation. (2) 50% of the estate tax goes to the central government, 20% to the provinces, and 30% to the counties and cities (30% for special cities, and the rest goes to the central government) for allocation. (3) The slaughter tax and tooth sticker tax are entirely allocated to the cities and counties. (4) The property of temples and monasteries is allocated to the counties and cities or local organizations according to their origin. (5) The education surcharge on land tax is entirely allocated to the counties and cities. (6) The education surcharge on tobacco and alcohol tax is allocated 50% to the provinces and 50% to the counties and cities. (7) The income of various education surcharges and taxes that originally existed in the local area will be handled as usual, unless otherwise stipulated by laws and regulations. (B) Income partially used for education funding (1) Gengkuan and its investment income. (2) Production taxes (such as tea tax and cocoon tax). (3) Consumption taxes (such as banquet tax and entertainment tax). (4) House tax and shop tax. (5) Business tax (6) The distribution of income tax above a certain percentage will be determined separately. (C) Determination of the principle of central subsidies for education funds (1) The original education funds of provinces, cities, and counties should still be allocated for the original education undertakings. (2) Provinces and cities should allocate 30% of the newly added education tax revenue for compulsory education and adult supplementary education funding, and cities and counties should allocate 80% for compulsory education and adult supplementary education funding. (3) When the education funding for compulsory education and adult supplementary education in counties and cities is insufficient, the provinces should make up the amount. (4) When the education funding for compulsory education and adult supplementary education in provinces is insufficient, the central government should make up the amount. (5) The central government should bear at least 45% of the total amount of compulsory education and adult supplementary education funding. (6) When the central government's portion of the income in the above two categories is insufficient to the prescribed amount, the Ministry of Finance should allocate it from the central government's general income. (7) The compulsory education and adult supplementary education funding allocated by the central government should be allocated by the Ministry of Education in detail according to the needs of each province,

city, and county.

(C) The principle of independence of education funding should be re-determined.

It goes without saying that it is the legacy of the Prime Minister that education funding should be guaranteed its independence. According to the principle of independence of education funding, a special accounting system should be adopted. Once local tax revenue designated for education funding is determined, it cannot be transferred to other uses. Once central tax revenue designated for education funding is determined, it cannot be transferred to other uses. Only in this way can the entire education plan be implemented. Only in this way can the development of China's education cause have hope.

Administrative Talk Meeting To Be Held Tomorrow Morning 95

▲ Convened by the Ministry of Education

▲ Three Discussion Points

On the morning of the 24th, the Ministry of Education will convene education administrative authorities from various provinces and municipalities for an administrative talk meeting in the Ministry's conference room. The purpose is to understand the obstacles in the educational administration of various provinces and municipalities, to find ways to avoid them, and to ensure the smooth implementation of the education plan. The main issues for discussion are: (1) Education statistics: some provinces and municipalities have submitted complete reports, some have submitted incomplete reports, and some have not yet submitted reports. What are the obstacles preventing unified and timely reporting? A detailed discussion is required. (2) Implementation of the compulsory education plan: now that the plan has been resolved by the National Education Conference, all provinces and municipalities must implement it within the specified time limit. However, what obstacles are there during implementation? Advantage can be taken of the presence in Beijing of education authorities from various provinces and municipalities for detailed discussion. (3) Promotion of the phonetic alphabet, and other discussions. The meeting will last for half a day. Various departments of the Ministry of Education had pre-prepared proposals but due to limited time, some were effectively cancelled.
