Conversation with Yang Zhongming, Representative of the Anhui Education Department 98

▲ Details of Education in Anhui Province

▲ Divided into Seven Major Items

Mr. Yang Zhongming, representative of the Anhui Provincial Education Department, currently the Chief of the Third Section and concurrently the Chief of the Fourth Section of the Department, arrived in Beijing late on the 15th and stayed at the Central Hotel. The reporter had previously visited him and learned that Director Cheng originally intended to attend the education conference in person to earnestly discuss practical educational issues with various educators. However, due to concurrently holding the position of Chairman and being extremely busy, he instructed the representative to attend. He was commissioned by the provincial government to go to Hangzhou to visit the National Games and returned to Anhui through Beijing on the 13th. He came to Beijing from Anhui again on the 14th. Due to delays in the ship, he did not attend the opening ceremony. He also talked in detail about the education situation in Anhui. Therefore, Mr. Yang's conversation is described in detail below in separate sections:

(1) Education Funding

The provincial education funding in Anhui Province was originally allocated from the provincial treasury and local taxes at a rate of 100,000 yuan per month. After the Jiang Gaoqi case occurred in 1921, it was increased from 950,000 to 1,530,000 yuan. However, it was often affected by finance and could not be paid according to the budget. The actual expenditure was still no more than 1,200,000 yuan. In April 1927, the National Revolutionary Army settled Anhui, and the Political Committee decided to use the cigarette tax designated as education funds in 1923 to fully fund education. In July of the same year, the Central Financial Conference decided that cigarette tax revenue should be managed centrally and that land tax should be used as education funds. After strong arguments from the education sector, the provincial government agreed with the Ministry of Finance to allocate 30% of the cigarette tax to education funds on a monthly basis. When the Ministry of Finance changed the cigarette tax collection method in February 1934 to a one-time unified collection at the time of import, and provinces could no longer levy taxes, Anhui's education funds were again shaken. After repeated strong arguments from the entire education sector, and the provincial government commissioned the directors of the Finance and Education Departments to come to Beijing to discuss compensation measures, after several consultations, the Ministry of Finance agreed to allocate 100,000 yuan per month to make up for the shortfall, which was still funded by provincial local taxes. Since Director Cheng took office, various education undertakings have been gradually expanded, and education funding has also been increased from 1,350,000 yuan to 1,700,000 yuan. Together with the provincial university funding of 700,000 yuan, the actual annual expenditure is as high as 2,400,000 yuan, which is not easy to achieve in one year. Most of the education funding in various counties is stretched, with the highest not exceeding 100,000 yuan and the lowest less than 3,000 yuan. Most of the sources come from school land and land tax surcharges. Since former Director Han actively cleaned up and Director Cheng worked hard to increase funding, except for a few counties that have not yet submitted reports, the total amount has increased from more than 540,000 yuan to more than 1.1 million yuan. In addition, in order to promote compulsory education, the Provincial Education Administrative Conference in 1922 resolved to levy six surcharges on farmland, livestock slaughter, tooth certificates, real estate registration, and cigarette and wine excise taxes as special funds for compulsory education. However, many counties have requested reductions, exemptions, or postponement of implementation due to years of famine or military impact.

(2) Higher Education

Anhui University first recruited preparatory classes in the spring of 1928, which was the beginning of the university's establishment. In the autumn of the same year, it enrolled students and opened the Faculties of Arts and Law. In the spring of 1929, it was taken over and reorganized by the provincial government, renamed Anhui Provincial University, and hired Director Cheng to concurrently serve as the president. Various regulations were formulated, books and instruments were purchased, and the Faculty of Science was prepared. During the summer vacation, Director Cheng resigned from his concurrent position as president, and the provincial government hired Mr. Wang Xinggong as the president, increased funding, and officially recruited science students. Last semester, there were 133 faculty and staff members and 401 students. As for studying abroad, Anhui has two types of provincial-funded students and scholarship students. There are 32 places for provincial-funded students, and 70 places for scholarship students. The annual tuition fee for the former varies depending on the country, while the annual allowance for the latter is about half of the tuition fee for provincial-funded students. After Director Cheng took office in the winter of 1928, he reviewed the Anhui provincial examinations for provincial-funded students in Europe and the United States, and found that they had not been held. In recent years, there have been vacancies for many graduates who have returned to China after studying abroad, which urgently need to be filled. Therefore, an overseas student examination was held in July last year, and a total of seven students were selected, all of whom have been sent abroad one after another. Furthermore, in accordance with the regulations for awarding scholarships to self-funded students, about 20 East and West Ocean scholarship students have been reviewed and supplemented. In addition, annual subsidies are provided to 180 outstanding students from Anhui Province who are enrolled in national universities and private prestigious universities registered with the Ministry of Education, with an annual award of 110 yuan per person.

(3) Secondary Education

Since the reorganization of Anhui Provincial Secondary Schools in 1927, there have been six middle schools, one junior high school, four girls' middle schools, two girls' middle schools in preparation, and five secondary vocational schools. After Director Cheng took office, he worked hard to expand them, expanding Wuhu Junior High School into the Seventh Middle School, and the Fifth and Sixth Girls' Middle Schools were also formally established one after another. A Fourth Secondary Vocational School was established in Bengbu, and a Rural Normal School was added in Guichi. According to statistics, there are currently 20 provincial secondary schools with 142 classes. Together with public and private secondary schools, there are 64 schools with 284 classes. All expenses account for 60% of the total education expenses.

(4) Elementary Education

Under the provincial education undertakings, in addition to the experimental primary schools of various middle schools and the primary schools in Anqing City, which were originally provincial-funded and directly under the jurisdiction of the Education Department, the rest are handled by various counties. According to a survey conducted last spring, excluding two counties that did not submit reports, the total number of schools was 3,369 and the number of students was 121,088. Active promotion has been carried out in the past year, and the number should be more than this. Regarding primary school teachers, the qualification of primary school Party Ideology teachers has been tested, and it has been stipulated that primary schools should give priority to hiring normal school graduates. Regarding the investigation of school-age children, in addition to the provincial capital, which has been completed, other counties are actively carrying out the work. Regarding Party Scout education, in addition to investigating the organizational status of various cities and counties and promulgating various regulations, the scout troops of primary schools in the provincial capital have undergone several reviews and performances and have achieved considerable results. In addition, the promotion of kindergarten education, the organization of primary education research associations, and the compilation of statistics on various other education undertakings are all actively underway.

(5) Compulsory Education

This year's work, regarding administrative aspects, the organizational outline of the Compulsory Education Committee of each city and county was formulated, and each city and county was ordered to quickly organize a Compulsory Education Committee. Regarding funding, regulations for the collection, management, and distribution of compulsory education surcharges were formulated to solemnly ensure special funds for compulsory education. Regarding

Page 12

Regarding teachers, regulations for the training of compulsory education teachers and temporary regulations for the examination of teachers were formulated to cultivate compulsory education teachers. Regarding research and planning, a book of opinions on the vigorous implementation of compulsory education in Anhui was compiled, methods for researching and investigating school-age children were studied, and an outline of the entire work of the vigorous implementation of compulsory education in Anhui was planned. In addition, the establishment of rural normal schools and the increase in compulsory education funds are all matters related to the implementation of compulsory education this year.

(6) Social Education

The social education institutions run by the province include three popular education centers, located in Anqing, Wuhu, and Bengbu. Among them, the First Popular Education Center is larger in scale, and is divided into five departments: promotion of books, museums, recreational arts, and sports. It also runs municipal movie theaters, children's playgrounds, public reading rooms, and public schools. The provincial library, also located in Anqing, has a large collection of Chinese and Western books. In addition, regarding the social education institutions established in various counties, there are 66 institutions in 36 counties, most of which are difficult to develop due to funding issues. It has now been stipulated that county-level social education institutions that have been operating for two years with excellent results and lack funding may be subsidized by provincial funds as appropriate.

(7) Mass Education

In the autumn of 1928, in order to promote mass education and cultivate teachers for mass schools, former Director Han established the Mass Education Normal Training Institute, ordering each county to send two primary school teachers and people with mass education interests to the institute to study. After Director Cheng took office, he completed the work and revised the organizational outline of the Anhui Provincial Mass Education Committee, ordering each county to organize a mass education committee and actively promote it. It is now found that 44 counties have established mass education committees, and each county has up to 41 mass schools. In addition, this Department and the organs of the provincial capital also run many mass schools to promote them.

In short, Anhui education has been striving to rectify and expand in the past year. In addition to the above, such as convening the Provincial Education Bureau Chiefs' Conference, the Provincial Secondary School Principals' Conference, holding the Education Bureau Chiefs' Examination, the Overseas Student Examination, opening summer schools and summer academic lecture meetings, testing Party Ideology teachers, holding the Provincial Student Speech Contest, the Provincial Games, and continuing to hold the Fourth Central China Games, as well as the Education Research Association for research and the Achievement Exhibition for learning, if this continues unabated, the people of Anhui, who have always been known for lagging behind in education, may have hope of catching up.

Health Education by Jin Baoshan 99

▲ Must emphasize health education

▲ Cultivate teachers for primary and secondary schools

▲ Should establish standardized teaching materials

The other day, at the Fourth General Assembly, during the discussion of the elementary education plan, regarding Article 9 on health education, Jin Baoshan advocated for specialized training to cultivate suitable talent. At that time, both Wei Que and Yu Ziyi supported his proposal. The matter of submitting Jin's written suggestions to the editing section of the assembly for revision, etc., was reported in yesterday's newspaper. Here, we extract Jin's written suggestions as follows:

Health education is a new global movement since the European War. Modern hygienists and educators believe that health and education are mutually beneficial and indispensable. Education is life, and health is the state of life that enables individuals to make the greatest social contribution. During the war, physical examinations of recruits in various countries revealed many physical defects, proving the weakness of using laws to promote health. It became clear that a rich life enabling the greatest social contribution depends entirely on individual habits, attitudes, and appreciation. However, to achieve this goal, education is essential. Health, as one of the most important goals of education, has been generally recognized by educators worldwide. The World Federation of Education Associations established a health education group from its inception. In recent years, both public and private health education institutions in various locations have seen the experimentation, demonstrations, research, and talent development related to health education flourish like bamboo shoots after rain. Any country seeking progress cannot isolate itself from this movement with profound significance for humanity.

Health education in our country is even more necessary than in other countries. The ignorance and superstition of the general public are significant causes of the current poor health situation. Economic poverty, lack of scientific medicine, inconvenient transportation, vast land, and a large population cannot lead to improved health conditions without starting with education. Laws alone are difficult to extend to the entire population. To take a step back, if the public lacks adequate education to feel the need for health and understand its value, then all public health construction will lack a foundation. The largest cause of death in our country is gastrointestinal infectious diseases. In other civilized countries, such diseases have been almost completely eradicated through public health measures. However, in our country, general health construction is not permitted by economic conditions, and the number of scientific physicians is so small that there is no better method than individual education to enable the general public to know how to avoid them. Based on this point alone, it is sufficient to prove the extraordinary importance of health education in our country.

The cultivation of habits, attitudes, and appreciation must begin in childhood, which goes without saying. Therefore, health facilities in schools are a major step in health education. As a result, the Ministry of Education of the National Government has included health as a subject in its recently promulgated curriculum standards for primary and secondary schools. However, teachers and teaching materials remain important issues. Without proper solutions, good health education in primary and secondary schools is impossible. In the past, those responsible for health education in primary and secondary schools generally lacked specialized training. The teaching methods and materials they used mostly emphasized human physiology and anatomy. The meaning and training of health habits, healthcare, and disease prevention were often neglected, failing to meet the trends of modern health education. To achieve fundamental improvement, the cultivation of teachers and the establishment of standardized teaching materials are urgent tasks.

To cultivate teachers for primary and secondary schools, health education should be included as a required course in the curriculum of normal schools, senior high school normal departments, rural normal schools, or normal training institutes. To cultivate teachers for secondary normal schools, health education departments or specialized health education programs should be established in university education colleges and normal colleges. The proposed system table for cultivating health education teachers at all levels is as follows:

Health Education Teacher System Table

Junior High School Health Curriculum

Health Education Department Health Education Curriculum for Senior High School Normal Department

University Graduate School University Education College Normal College Elementary Schools and Kindergartens

Specialized Health Education Program Normal School Health Education Curriculum

Rural Normal School Health Education Curriculum Social studies and natural science courses, as well as various other courses, should all include the meaning of health education.

As a temporary solution to meet current needs, short-term training should be provided for current or prospective primary and secondary school health teachers. Examples include the summer health education workshops organized by the Ministries of Education and Health last summer, and the elementary school teacher health education workshops organized by the city of Beiping this spring. Inviting experts to give lectures and conduct experiments is also quite convenient. If local education authorities can find ways to organize these, their contribution to the future of health education will certainly not be insignificant. Regarding the establishment of standardized teaching materials, attention should be paid to the following key points:

1. The health curriculum for primary schools should focus on developing children's health habits. Only a few examples of physiology and anatomy need to be briefly explained.

2. The health curriculum for junior high schools, in addition to developing health habits, should also cover the general principles of human physiology and anatomy, as well as preventive medicine and social hygiene.

3. The health curriculum for senior high schools must be taught in conjunction with civics, biology, home economics, and physical education.

Detailed standards for health curriculum in primary and secondary schools have been specified in the first and second volumes of the Ministry of Education's Provisional Curriculum Standards for Primary and Secondary Schools (regarding kindergartens and primary schools, see pages 6 to 8 of the first volume in the social studies and natural science course, pages 45 to 47 in the primary school social studies course, and pages 54 to 56 in the primary school natural science course; regarding junior high schools, see pages 103 to 108 of the second volume in the provisional curriculum standards for junior high school physiology and hygiene), which can be consulted. There is no need to repeat them here.

Senior high school normal departments and normal schools are important institutions for cultivating primary and secondary school teachers. Special attention should be paid to the health education course. Its curriculum standards have been drafted in conjunction with Comrade Yuan Dunli and submitted to the Ministry of Education for adoption by the Curriculum Standards Committee (the draft standards are omitted).

The curriculum for specialized health education programs in university education colleges and normal colleges should also be drafted carefully to serve as a blueprint for future implementation. The main points are described below: Required courses: Chinese and English, 6 credits each; biology and physiology, 4 credits each, each with 3 hours of lecture and 3 hours of experiment; personal hygiene, 4 credits; microbiology and nutrition, 4 credits each, each with 3 hours of lecture and 2 hours of experiment; health education, 6 credits; philosophy of education, principles of teaching, educational psychology, and physical education, 4 credits each; internship to be determined, totaling 56 credits. Elective courses: Maternal and child hygiene, 4 credits; mental hygiene and home nursing, 2 credits each; and psychology, sociology, educational administration, educational testing and statistics, principles of physical education, and other courses, for a total of 24 elective credits, totaling 80 credits for graduation.

Health Education Department Curriculum (University students can choose health education as a major or minor subject. This curriculum should be determined based on individual interests.) Only the following three courses are required: 1. Personal Hygiene, 4 credits; 2. Public Health, 2 credits; 3. Health Education, 6 credits. The remaining credits should be selected from other courses in the specialized program.

University Graduate School Curriculum: All subjects related to health education can be studied. The duration is indefinite.

A Few Opinions on Normal Education by Cheng Tianfang 100

The main purpose of normal education is to cultivate sound teachers, both morally and academically, through appropriate scientific education and rigorous physical and mental training. Therefore, normal education is the foundation of a country's education. The normal education system should occupy an important position in the entire academic system. Our country's normal education has never had a sound system. Since the implementation of the new academic system, the normal education system has become increasingly fragmented and dysfunctional. In the Seventeenth National Education Conference, the reorganization of the normal education system was one of the central issues of the conference. As a result of the discussions, although the majority supported the principle of "independent normal education" and resolved that "in order to promote compulsory education," independent normal schools or normal training institutes should be established in various provinces to specially train primary school teachers in addition to senior high school normal departments," there was no detailed provision for the entire normal education system and the implementation plan for normal education. Therefore, the normal education problem, which was the focus of attention in the national education community, was not thoroughly resolved. Now, the National Education Conference is meeting again in the capital. Chapter 3 of the entire education plan of this National Education Conference is specifically about the "Plan for Establishing Teacher Training Institutions at All Levels and of All Types." In that draft plan, there are various detailed plans for the goals, duration, level, years, school establishment methods, curriculum outline, internship methods, service and treatment, teacher recruitment methods for primary and secondary schools, and vocational teacher training methods of normal education. One point that deserves our attention the most is that in this plan, normal education (i.e., teacher training institutions at all levels) has been established as an integrated system. The spirit of independent normal education has been very clearly expressed. Now that the National Education Conference has been in session for some time, there should be a more detailed discussion on the issue of normal education. As I am unable to personally attend the grand meeting due to other commitments, I would like to briefly describe my personal opinions on normal education for reference.

(1) Opinions on the Normal Education System

(1) Normal education bears the mission of cultivating teachers at all levels and is the foundation of education at all levels. Therefore, normal education at all levels should form an independent and complete system to avoid a lack of standards and a diverse content. (2) Normal education is a national undertaking and an important tool for building the country through education. The location of schools, the number of teachers cultivated, the policies for rewarding teachers, and the methods for training teachers should all be determined by the government according to the needs of the times and the environment. Therefore, normal schools at all levels should be established by the public sector to avoid each acting on its own and losing the true meaning of normal education. American educator Professor Proi Bagley said that the administration of normal education should be based on the national level, or at least on the provincial level. This is the reason.

(3) In the secondary education stage, the two systems of secondary school normal departments and normal schools can coexist without conflict. However, each province should establish at least one complete normal school. In the future, the establishment of new normal schools in various provinces and counties should also be based on independent operation in order to concentrate training, clarify goals, and easily cultivate normal school students' interest and attitude in viewing education as a profession.

(4) Cultivating rural teachers is a prerequisite for promoting rural education. Therefore, provinces, cities, and counties should widely establish rural normal schools to cultivate rural teachers. The funding should be borne by the counties and cities, but the central and provincial governments should investigate the financial strength of the counties and cities and provide adequate subsidies.

(2) Opinions on the Curriculum of Normal Schools

(1) The curriculum of normal schools at all levels should pay attention to two aspects: general training and professional training. The main purpose of the first type of training is to improve personality and enrich life. The main purpose of the second type of training is to increase teaching efficiency.

(2) The curriculum organization of normal schools at all levels should be centered on the actual activities of the school. For example, the curriculum of kindergarten normal schools should be centered on the actual activities of kindergartens, and the curriculum of rural normal schools should be centered on the actual activities of rural primary schools.

(3) The curriculum of normal schools at all levels should focus on cultivating normal students' attitude and enjoyment of viewing education as a profession.

(4) The curriculum of normal schools at all levels should be formulated by the Ministry of Education organizing a curriculum standards drafting committee, which should promulgate and implement the standards. However, the curriculum standards should be flexible and leave room for local activities.

(3) Opinions on the Internship Methods for Normal School Students

(1) The internship of normal school students should at least pay attention to the following three aspects: teaching internship, discipline management internship, and administrative internship.

(2) Normal schools should organize a teaching internship committee to be responsible for guiding the teaching internship.

(3) The internship time for normal school students should be extended as much as possible, and the internship results should be given special attention. Normal school students who fail the internship should not be given a graduation certificate or be allowed to serve as school teachers, regardless of their academic performance.

(4) Opinions on the Treatment Methods for Normal School Students

Normal education is the source of national education. Normal school graduates bear the important mission of directly training the next generation of citizens. Therefore, normal schools should adopt a public funding system. Normal school students should enjoy the right to be exempted from tuition and accommodation fees while at school. However, the service period after graduation should also be clearly stipulated to prevent abuses.

The above are all important issues of normal education today. Because the Shen Bao is publishing a special issue on the National Education Conference, the Shen Bao reporter asked me for contributions. Therefore, I would like to simply contribute a few of my personal opinions on normal education, hoping that all the participants of the National Education Conference will discuss this issue related to the foundation of the country in more detail.

Boy Scouts hold memorial week in front of Dr. Sun Yat-sen's Mausoleum - Dai Jitao's speech

(Photo taken in Nanjing Guanghua)

Anecdotes from the Conference 101

▲ Personal Issues: During yesterday's discussion of the higher education plan, regarding the article on professor class time, those who supported and those who opposed concurrent teaching debated for a long time. Some said that this article was related to the self-interest of the members, so they had to argue for it. As a result, professors were divided into two types: full-time and part-time, to take into account the opinions of all parties.

▲ Hair Statistics: Of the 87 members who attended yesterday, 49 had parted hair or combed it back, 35 had monk heads or flat tops, and 3 were bald, with slightly longer hair around the perimeter to show that they were not slick.

▲ School Photography: During the conference, the members' postures can be divided into several types: some are focused and attentive to the discussion of the proposals, some are leaning on the table and dozing off, some are good at drawing and have drawn several good paintings by the time the conference is over, and some are reading various books and newspapers that they have obtained unexpectedly, with great interest. This is the phenomenon of students in middle school and above during class. Most educators who are old hands at teaching are unconsciously influenced by them and reflect it unintentionally.

National Boy Scout General Review Concludes 102

The chairman delivered a speech at the award ceremony yesterday

The closing ceremony of the first National Boy Scout General Review and Jamboree of China was held at 9:00 am on the 21st in the auditorium of the Central Military Academy. All the Boy Scout Central Committee members and representatives of the calling agencies, guests, etc., totaling three to four thousand people, attended, presided over by Chairman Dai Jitao. The situation is recorded as follows:

Attendees 103

Shao Yuancong, Zhu Lihuo, Zhang Nanxian, Liu Ruiheng, Ding Chaowu, Zhang Yezhong, Gui Chongji, Zhou Yawei, Zhu Maocheng, Kong Xiangxi, Chiang Kai-shek, Dai Jitao, Shi Weihuan, Zhang Daofan, and representatives and guests from various agencies, etc.

Venue Arrangement 104

In the center of the stage, the portrait of Sun Yat-sen and the flag of the party and the country were hung. At the entrance of the hall, registration desks were set up on both sides. In the hall, there were seats for newspaper reporters on both sides of the stage, and the guests were in the center. The Boy Scouts were arranged by position, but because of the large number of people, the hall was full of Boy Scouts on all sides and upstairs. The order in the hall was maintained by 20 groups of Girl Scouts with batons, and the order was well maintained.

Closing Order 105

(1) All stand at attention; (2) Play music; (3) Sing the Party song; (4) Bow three times to the Party flag, the national flag, and the portrait of Sun Yat-sen; (5) The chairman respectfully reads Sun Yat-sen's will; (6) Three minutes of silence; (7) Sing the Boy Scout song; (8) The chairman delivers the closing speech; (9) Central Committee members give instructions; (10) Guests give speeches; (11) Cheers: 1. Long live the Boy Scouts of China; 2. Long live the Chinese Kuomintang; 3. Long live the National Government; 4. Long live the Republic of China; 5. Long live the Three Principles of the People, long live, long live, long live; (12) Play music; (13) Ceremony completed.

Chairman Chiang Attends 106

Chairman Chiang was originally scheduled to go to Hankou for a review at 8:00 am, but he postponed it by two or three hours because he had to attend the closing ceremony. Around 10:00 am, Chiang arrived by car. After entering the venue, he went to the rest area to rest. Chiang was wearing a military uniform with a smile on his face.

Shi Weihuan Reports 107

It was briefly stated that today's closing ceremony was originally scheduled to be held at 9:00 am. Now, because the number of prizes and souvenirs donated by various parties is about 20,000, it is planned to distribute them separately at the closing ceremony. Now, Chairman Dai and the staff of the Central Committee Office, etc., are discussing the prize distribution method, which will take about 120 minutes to complete. Please wait a moment for all the Boy Scouts and guests, etc.

Number of Prizes 108

The number of prizes and souvenirs donated by various parties this time is extremely large. As of the closing date, there are still items being delivered one after another, totaling more than 20,000 souvenirs. Each group can get seven or eight copies. Each Boy Scout and staff member can get four or five or seven or eight items. There are also about one or two hundred types of prizes, totaling more than one thousand items.

Each group can get three or four items.

Chairman Chiang's Speech 109

▲ Save the country and the people with doctrine

▲ Work together to resist foreign aggression

At 10:30, Chiang delivered a speech to the entire audience from the stage because he had to go to Xiaguan to board a ship to Hankou. All the Boy Scouts applauded when they saw Chiang. Chiang nodded with a smile as a greeting and then delivered the following speech:

Comrades, before the meeting, I was about to board the ship. I can't wait for the meeting, so I will say a few words to you and say goodbye. The Boy Scout General Review and Jamboree has been held until today and has come to a close. Our Boy Scouts have achieved very good results, which is really the best sign of the success of the Chinese revolution. At the same time, because of this General Review, the success of the revolution will definitely be faster. Therefore, our National Government's committee members and all party members and citizens have endless hopes for this General Review, because your achievements and results can increase the strength of the party, can increase the courage of party members and soldiers, and be your vanguard to defeat the warlords and imperialism. At the same time, it makes the warlords afraid and imperialism tremble. You are all very young, some are only ten years old, and the oldest is only about twenty years old. Now you can gather more than 3,000 people, which encourages party members and soldiers to be brave. If you are twenty to thirty years old and gather 30,000 or 50,000 people, your strength will be greater and the success will be faster. You have no guns or cannons, so how can you make the warlords and imperialism afraid? Because you have no selfish desires, no desire to sacrifice others for yourself, so Boy Scouts are the treasure of the country. If,

Without Boy Scouts, the country has no foundation and no new life, so you must be the new life of the country and should take on the new cause of the country. From now on, all Boy Scouts should cherish the glory of the Boy Scouts, protect the reputation and discipline of the Boy Scouts, and work together to unite the warlords and fight together, live and die together. If you can do this, as long as there are thirty people in a group, you can defeat the warlords and make them tremble. The reason why China is bullied by foreigners is because we cannot unite. In the past, we were successful in uniting today, but tomorrow we will destroy the group organization due to conflicts of interest. Therefore, foreigners look down on us. In the future, people should unite, love each other, and live and die together. In this way, our 3,000 Boy Scouts can oppress 30,000 rebellious troops. I hope that you will pay attention to the group, protect the reputation of the group, and sacrifice everything in order to be a complete Boy Scout. We know that unity is difficult, and it is even more difficult to live and die together. We should know why we want to live and die together, because the revolution has a doctrine, and the doctrine is to save the country and the people. This doctrine is the Three Principles of the People. If the Three Principles of the People can succeed, foreigners will not dare to bully people. If not, our China will perish. Therefore, I hope that you will work together to consistently implement the Three Principles of the People. If one person in your group is bullied by foreigners, the whole group will unite to support them. Therefore, if you Boy Scouts can sacrifice for the doctrine, then the power of the doctrine will be greater. If the doctrine cannot be implemented, the extinction of the race and the invasion of foreign enemies are all worrying. Therefore, everyone should love each other, like hands and feet, and recognize that only the doctrine can save the country and the people. We should fight for the doctrine, and then the Boy Scouts will have power. At the same time, to make the doctrine show power, we must realize the doctrine. Everyone fights for the doctrine and joins the party. I believe that when 3,000 Boy Scouts join our party and become followers of Sun Yat-sen, Sun Yat-sen in heaven will definitely laugh heartily, because Sun Yat-sen most hopes that Chinese youth can achieve this goal today and can be happy and gratified. Today, I hope that you will not only support our party, but also join our party. Everyone should understand that without a party, we cannot unite. Without a party, the revolution cannot succeed. Therefore, I hope that you will work together to fight for the doctrine and consistently listen to the orders of our party to defeat all the warlords, and then the revolution can succeed. Because I have to go to Hankou immediately, I cannot talk in detail. At the same time, I have a proposal. The age for joining our party must be over sixteen years old. Now I plan to find a special way that, regardless of age, all Boy Scouts can be probationary party members. But after joining the party, you are followers of Sun Yat-sen and cannot be casual. You should fight for the party and win glory for the party. In this way, the revolution can succeed and you can also succeed. I especially hope that girls will also join and fight for the party together, so that China can achieve independence and freedom as soon as possible and abolish unequal treaties. I hope that you will sacrifice for the doctrine and wish you all good health and success. Finished.

Meeting Situation 110

At 11 o'clock, the meeting started with music. Chairman Dai Jitao led the ceremony and sang the Boy Scout song. Then, Chairman Dai delivered the closing speech, followed by Central Committee member Shao Yuancong's instructions, and then speeches by guests, including Zhang Ximan, Zhou Yawei, and Zhang Zhizhong. Finally, Gu Zheng, a representative elected by the Boy Scouts, gave a reply, and Zhang Daofan reported on the award method. After the report, a lottery was held, and Mrs. Chiang Kai-shek, Soong Mei-ling, gave the awards. It was not completed until the afternoon. Then, everyone cheered, played music, and dispersed.

Chairman's Speech 111

Chairman Dai Chuanxian delivered a speech, saying that the central government's national Boy Scout inspection and jamboree these past few days have shown that the Boy Scout troops have made excellent progress in organization and education during the first inspection. The service members, troop leaders, and individual Boy Scouts, both brothers and sisters, have all shown great spirit. He is very pleased that everyone is gathered here today for the closing ceremony. Since this inspection, the organization has been unified. Now, he will briefly explain his feelings and impressions of this general inspection. During this inspection, we have gained profound experience. At the same time, we have brought together Boy Scouts from various provinces and cities in the north, south, east, and west to unite with each other. The regret is that Boy Scout Commander He Yingqin is currently leading a large army to suppress the rebellion and could not return to the capital, so the swearing-in ceremony for the commander could not be held as scheduled. Also, due to the uncertain weather, there were many difficulties in running the event. Furthermore, due to the incomplete construction of Nanjing, the meeting venues, training grounds, and camping grounds were not fully equipped. However, human effort can overcome nature. He hopes that all comrades will uphold the spirit of fearlessness and resist according to the motto that human determination can conquer nature. Moreover, there are several points we should strive for in the future: (1) The uniforms, flags, badges, etc., of each troop should be uniform and standardized. (2) Discipline must be strict, and etiquette must be solemn. (3) The ability to appreciate music is essential. He will also briefly report on the method of distributing prizes. Regarding the prizes, the designated winners will be reserved for next year's distribution. This year's awards will be determined by drawing lots, without distinction of merit. However, Boy Scouts from faraway places and vocational groups will receive a little more from the organizing committee as encouragement. There will also be special prizes for young children and Girl Scouts. In general, each troop will receive seven items in total, and each person will receive five items.

Guest Speeches 112

After Dai Chuanxian's closing remarks, Shao Yuanchong, representative of the Central Party Headquarters, Zhang Ximan of the Ministry of Education, Zhou Yawei, Deputy Director of the Training Directorate, and Zhang Zhizhong, Education Director of the Central Military Academy, successively delivered speeches with much encouragement. Finally, Gu Zheng, representative of the Boy Scouts, responded.

Method of Drawing Lots 113

After the speeches, Zhang Daofan reported on the method of drawing lots, stating that the prizes were divided into different grades. For the drawing of lots, two of the youngest Boy Scouts, one male and one female, were selected from among the Girl Scouts to come forward and draw lots. The size of each troop's winnings depends on its luck.

Situation of Drawing Lots 114

During the drawing of lots, each troop nominated the youngest male and female Boy Scouts to participate. The male was Liu Enyun (9 years old) from the 80th Troop, and the female was Wu Zongshu (11 years old) from the 195th Troop. After being nominated, Liu and Wu went on stage to draw lots separately.

Prize Giving 115

On this day, the prize giving was presided over by Madame Song Meiling, wife of the Chairman of the National Government. After each troop drew its prize number, Song distributed the prizes separately on stage. A representative from each winning troop came to the front of the stage to receive the number and then went to the Officer Research Class to collect the prize based on the number.

Forming Up to Return to Camp 116

After the distribution of prize numbers was completed, it was 2:00 PM. The closing ceremony was then announced, and the Boy Scout troops successively formed up and returned to camp.

Random Notes from the Camp 119

▲ He Yingqin's Telegram to Boy Scouts Nationwide

(Above excerpt) The responsibility of saving the country lies heavily on the youth. Coming from afar to the capital to receive inspection, their spirits are uplifted, which serves as a model for the nation's youth. I am deeply fortunate and pleased. Yingqin and Yan and Feng are creating chaos, and the warlords are putting up a stubborn resistance. I have been ordered to come to Hankou to oversee the military operations of suppressing the rebellion, so I cannot return to the capital as scheduled to attend the grand ceremony, which I deeply regret. I hereby extend my apologies via telegram and wish you all good health and continued progress.

▲ Performance of China's New Flag Semaphore

Among the curriculum demonstrations of the Boy Scout Grand Inspection, the one most worthy of our attention seems to be "China's New Flag Semaphore." This was the first time "China's New Flag Semaphore" was performed independently. The topic was written and sealed by Central Committee member Dai Jitao, and the winners were the 5th Troop (Zhejiang Poor Children's Home) in first place and the 148th Troop (Zhejiang Provincial Rural Normal School) in second place. The time was 5 minutes and 34 seconds, and the phrase was "Comrades, unite and strive forward," a total of twelve characters. Each character took an average of 27.83 seconds. It is said that "China's New Flag Semaphore" was invented by Liu Zaoting, the principal of Zhejiang Provincial Rural Normal School, and personally tested in the 5th and 148th Troops. The 5th Troop is at the elementary school level, and the fact that it won the competition proves that this "China's New Flag Semaphore" is easy to understand. The second performance was a comparative experiment of "China's New Flag Semaphore" and other flag semaphores. According to the Guidance Department's plan, the participants were originally divided into two levels: middle school and elementary school. Unfortunately, apart from the 5th Troop's China New Flag Semaphore, there were no other participants from the elementary school level. Therefore, the competition was mixed, and the comparison standards were speed and accuracy. The test question was still set by Central Committee member Dai Jitao: "Boy Scouts must take the implementation of the Three Principles of the People as their mission," a total of fifteen characters. The result was that the 148th Troop came in first, with a time of 6 minutes and 5 seconds, averaging 24.23 seconds per character. The Troop came in second, with a time of 7 minutes and 5 seconds, averaging 31.40 seconds per character. Both of the above groups used "China's New Flag Semaphore" as their communication tool. The 155th Troop's telegraph code flag group ranked third, with a time of 12 minutes and 52 seconds, averaging 49.6 seconds per character, and the text was also correct. The 119th Troop's Nanyang English single flag group, although the time was close to 4 minutes and 8 seconds, averaging 16.53 seconds per character, translated the test question as "Boy Scouts implement the Three Principles of the People as his responsibility," so they ranked fourth. The 121st Troop's receiving station mistook the test question for "Boy Scouts should have the Three Principles of the People and the responsibility to serve the community." The 57th Troop's Shanghai Guangzhao Roman Phonetic Alphabet group ranked sixth with a time of 7 minutes, 17 and 4/5 seconds, averaging 29.18 seconds per character. The receiving station mistakenly translated the test question into "Boy Scouts must and the Three Principles of the People (illegible characters) line," an incomplete sentence. When the winning groups handed in their papers first, the central committee members nodded and praised them, and planned to add special rewards to promote them.

▲ Photo Presented by the Lishi Society

At the closing ceremony of the Boy Scouts, the Lishi Society printed a photo of President Chiang Kai-shek, with a small portrait of Chiang and the Lishi Society creed on the front, and a welcome message to all Boy Scouts on the back, which was distributed to all Boy Scout troops as a souvenir.

Important News

Organizational Outline of the Jiangsu Provincial and Municipal Compulsory Education Committee 121

Zhenjiang Express: The Jiangsu Provincial and Municipal Compulsory Education Committee's organizational outline was submitted to the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education for deliberation and was recently approved by the 286th provincial government meeting. The text is as follows: Article 1: This committee is organized in accordance with Article 10 of the Organizational Outline of the Central Compulsory Education Committee. Article 2: The purpose of this committee is to plan and promote the implementation of compulsory education in this county or city. Article 3: This committee is composed of the following personnel: A. Ex-officio members: one member of the county party committee, the county magistrate or mayor, the directors or heads and section chiefs of various county or city bureaus, one county or city school inspector, and the director of the school education section of the county or city education bureau. B. Appointed members: three to five people who have special experience or research in compulsory education shall be selected and appointed by the county or city education bureau. Article 4: The county magistrate or mayor shall be the chairman of this committee, and the director of the county education bureau shall be the vice chairman. Article 5: The affairs of this committee shall be concurrently managed by the staff of the county or city education bureau, and no additional salary or allowance shall be paid. Article 6: The powers of this committee are as follows: A. To plan the implementation of compulsory education in the entire county or city. B. To raise funds for the implementation of compulsory education in the entire county or city. C. To supervise the implementation of compulsory education in various districts, townships, and towns. Article 7: This committee shall hold a regular meeting once a month, convened by the chairman. Special meetings may be held when necessary. Article 8: When this committee holds a meeting, one representative from the provincial experimental primary school in this county or city may attend, and members of the education committee may also attend. Article 9: The resolutions of this committee shall be submitted by the county or city government to the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education for approval and implementation. Article 10: The expenses of this committee shall be paid from the county or city education funds and included in the budget. The budget standard shall be separately determined by the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education. Article 11: The members of this committee shall serve in a voluntary capacity, but appointed members may receive reimbursement for travel expenses when attending meetings. Article 12: This outline shall be submitted by the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education to the Jiangsu Provincial Government for approval and promulgation, and shall be sent to the Ministry of Education for record.

A Large Number of Visiting Groups from Liaoning Will Come to Shanghai 122

Since Liaoning returned to the central government, the provincial government has been determined to innovate in political construction. Commander Zhang Xueliang has paid more attention to education, and last autumn, he generously donated five million yuan to the primary and secondary school education foundation, and invited celebrities Yuan Jinkai, Wang Shuhan, and Liu Shangqing to be directors, in order to use the interest to run education and training schools. He also donated 200,000 yuan to open various Xinmin primary schools as a model for improving primary schools throughout the province. Recently, the provincial government subsidized the athletes participating in the National Games in Hangzhou with 20,000 yuan, and distributed 40,000 yuan to various school visiting groups, such as the 13-member visiting group of principals of provincial schools, led by Lin Yaoshan; the 34-member visiting group of Xinmin school principals, led by Jin Desen; the 55-member visiting group of primary school education research classes, guided by Lu Rixuan; the 18-member travel group of the Provincial Women's Normal School, led by Cai Weiqian; the 50-member visiting group of the Provincial No. 1 Normal School, led by Zhang Jinghan; the 40-member inspection group of the Provincial No. 3 Middle School, led by Yang Chunfeng; the 50-member visiting group of the Provincial No. 2 Normal School, led by Li Yinqing; the 20-member Tonghua education visiting group, led by Gao Pingu; the 20-member group personally led by Feng Yong; and the 14-member Harbin education inspection group, led by Li Yousheng. They have all gone south to Jiangsu and Zhejiang to inspect the work of education, politics, and the party, in order to learn from them. The president of the Education Association was specially hired as the general instructor, and Su Shangda and Qian Nianyao, two gentlemen from the Liaoning Chamber of Commerce, sent telegrams to Huang Jing in Shanghai to take care of everything.

News from the Far East Games 124

▲ Still Using Old Rules

The Chinese National Sports Association received a telegram from the Japanese Far East Games Preparatory Committee yesterday, stating that the competition rules for all sports in this Far East Games will be implemented in accordance with the rules set for the 8th Games, without any changes. The previous proposal to change the volleyball and swimming rules has now been cancelled.

▲ President Is Imperial Prince Chichibu

Dentsu, Tokyo, 22nd: The Japanese Sports Association has nominated Imperial Prince Chichibu as the president of the Far East Games. As a result of the coordination by the Sports Association's Equipment Committee, it has been decided that the decoration of the conference will be based on the national flags of China, Japan, and the Philippines.

▲ Selection of Chinese Team Emblem

The Chinese National Sports Association's solicitation for the emblem of the Chinese athletes for the Far East Games has been quite enthusiastic, with a total of more than 40 designs. The judging has now been completed, and the winning designs are: first place, Zhuang Jianzhang's shield-style red border, blue background, with a white sun and starburst in the center, the color is the same as the national emblem, and the appearance is very beautiful; second place, Gu Hongkui's plum blossom style; third place, Chen Zaixin's Great Wall double wing style.

▲ Participants From Eleven Schools

Long jump final, 8. 800-meter relay preliminary. Day 2: 1. 100-meter final, 2. Low hurdles semi-final, 3. Shot put final, 4. 400-meter final, 5. High hurdles final, 6. 200-meter semi-final, 7. Pole vault competition, 8. Javelin final, 9. 200-meter final, 10. Triple jump final, 11. Low hurdles final, 12. 800-meter final, 13. 800-meter relay final.

Local News

The Case of Resisting Chinese Directors 128

▲ Continued Efforts

The Shanghai Concession Chinese Ratepayers Association released the following information yesterday:

▲ Five Chinese Directors Question the Municipal Council The five newly appointed Chinese directors of the Municipal Council, Yuan Ludeng and others, recently sent a letter to Edward, the General Manager of the Municipal Council, stating: "Dear Sir, We, the undersigned, have been elected by the Shanghai Concession Chinese Ratepayers Association as directors to attend the Public Concession Municipal Council for this term, as notified by the association on April 16. With regard to the first board meeting on April 17, we did not receive any prior notice, and therefore could not attend. We hereby formally protest and reserve all rights to take appropriate action when necessary. We request your kind attention to this matter. Sincerely, Yuan Ludeng, Yu Qiaqing, Xu Xinliu, Bei Songsheng, Liu Hongsheng, April 19."

▲ Discussing the Basis for Increasing Chinese Directors Guowen News Agency reported: Yesterday, a well-known foreign legal expert in Shanghai talked about the declaration issued by the Shanghai Concession Chinese Ratepayers Association on April 18. It is not a fabrication. Although the declaration is based on principles, foreigners may think it is insignificant and think that they can refuse to recognize it or be bound by it. However, in reality, foreigners are bound by a kind of written law, namely, the Shanghai Foreign Settlement Regulations, also known as the Yangjingbang Regulations. Article 28 of the regulations states: "If it is necessary to modify or supplement these regulations in the future, and there are doubtful points in the various measures and powers stipulated in the regulations, the consuls of various countries and the local Chinese officials shall consult and revise them, and they shall be implemented only after they have been approved by the diplomatic corps and the Chinese government." Therefore, the addition or increase of Chinese directors to the Municipal Council is a "supplement" to the Settlement Regulations, which has been "consulted and approved by the consuls of various countries and the local Chinese officials and approved by the diplomatic corps and the Chinese government." Therefore, the Ratepayers Association has no right to discuss and resolve it.

▲ Municipal Party Department Resolves on Five Measures The Shanghai Special Municipal Executive Committee sent a letter to the Ratepayers Association yesterday, stating: "Dear Sir, The fact that the Ratepayers Association of the Public Concession of Shanghai has rejected the proposal to increase the number of Chinese directors this time is an infringement on sovereignty, and we share the same deep indignation. The following five measures have been resolved by this committee to deal with this situation: (1) Request the central government to order the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to actively recover the Shanghai Concession. (2) Before this committee has a proper solution, (2) The Chinese Ratepayers Association of the Concession should elect eleven additional directors to the municipal organs of the Concession and form its own board of directors to handle board affairs. (2) The taxes paid by the citizens of the Concession should be deposited uniformly in a bank designated by the Chinese Ratepayers Association from this month onwards and should no longer be remitted to the Municipal Council. (3) All properties owned by Chinese in the Concession that have obtained deed certificates by borrowing the names of foreign merchants should be cancelled and registered under the names of foreign merchants, and should be changed to the land administrative organs of our country.

(4) The Municipal Council should apologize to the Chinese directors for the rude and illegal actions of the Ratepayers Association. (5) Issue a declaration stating that the number of Chinese directors does not need to be approved by a special meeting of foreign taxpayers. Therefore, the claim that a special meeting of foreign taxpayers should be convened to seek remedies is not acceptable. In addition to the fact that (1) and (5) have already been handled, the remaining items (2, 3, and 4) should be investigated and handled by your association.

▲ Telegram from the Special Party Department of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways The Executive Committee of the Special Party Department of the Chinese Kuomintang on the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways sent a telegram to the Ratepayers Association, stating: "It has been reported that the Annual Meeting of Foreign Taxpayers in the Public Concession has rejected the issue of increasing the number of Chinese directors. We are deeply outraged. Shanghai is our Chinese territory, but due to the constraints of unequal treaties, our people have suffered endless humiliation. This rejection of the increase in Chinese directors is tantamount to gagging people and arbitrarily making decisions beyond one's authority, with the absurd intention of permanently occupying the Concession and not returning. If we continue to be complacent and do not strive for it, then there will never be room for Chinese people to speak in the Shanghai Concession, and there will never be hope of recovering the Concession. In addition to the fact that this committee has requested the central government to instruct the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to make a serious protest, we hereby request your association to rise up together, argue on the basis of reason, and strive to achieve legitimate goals, consolidate our national rights, and suppress the atrocities of imperialism, as a prelude to the recovery of rights. This committee respectfully leads the comrades of the two railways and pledges to be the rearguard. We are filled with urgency."

▲ Letter from the Yewenyi Road Business Federation The Yewenyi Road Ninth Road Business Federation sent a letter to the Ratepayers Association yesterday, stating: "Dear Sir, The Ratepayers Association of Foreign Taxpayers has exceeded its authority to discuss and reject the case of increasing the two Chinese directors of the Municipal Council. The merchants and citizens of our road are outraged by this. This matter concerns the rights of citizens. We hope that your association will continue its fearless spirit and strive to achieve its goals. The representatives of our association and the entire business community of this road are willing to be the rearguard and pledge to fight to the death with imperialism in order to avenge our humiliation and seek the realization of freedom and equality. We hereby send this letter for your information."

▲ The Ratepayers Association Replied to Four Organizations The Ratepayers Association replied to the Shanghai Municipal Party Department, the Shanghai County Party Department, the Special Party Department of the Two Railways, and the Yewenyi Road Ninth Road Business Federation yesterday, stating: "Dear Sir, The fact that the Shanghai Public Concession Foreign Taxpayers Association has exceeded its authority to reject the increase of two Chinese directors is a matter of deep indignation for all Chinese people. This association has formally issued declarations on the 17th and 18th of this month to express our views, and we deeply recognize that the rights that citizens should have cannot be firmly guaranteed unless the Concession is recovered. As for increasing the number of Chinese directors, it is only a compromise and a transitional measure before the Concession is recovered. On the one hand, it is a diplomatic issue, and on the other hand, it depends on the unanimous support of the people to achieve success. We are grateful for your association's expression of support and encouragement to strive for success. In the future, in addition to waiting for negotiations with the diplomatic authorities, we are also prepared to take legal and final measures when necessary to achieve our goals. We hereby send this reply and await your instructions."

▲ Declaration by the National Goods Maintenance Association The China National Goods Maintenance Association issued a declaration on the issue of the Western Directors of the Municipal Council, stating: "Fellow compatriots from all walks of life, please be advised that the proposal to increase the number of Chinese directors of the Public Concession Municipal Council has recently been rejected by the Annual Meeting of Foreign Taxpayers, and there have been speeches insulting all Chinese people. After reading this, we are shocked and indignant. We believe that Shanghai is our Chinese territory, and although it has been designated as a Concession due to temporary circumstances, the sovereignty lies with China, which is an indisputable principle. Moreover, Chinese residents still constitute the majority of the population in Shanghai, and the amount of taxes paid is also mostly paid by Chinese. According to the proportion of taxes paid, Chinese directors should also constitute the majority in order to be fair. Now, the Westerners living in Shanghai in the Public Concession regard themselves as the masters and act perversely to this extent. Moreover, the insulting remarks about the Chinese people in the reported speech are close to inciting hostility between China and foreign countries and destroying the spirit of cooperation, which is intolerable. We, the Chinese people who love peace, sincerely hope to work together with the municipal organs that have emerged from cooperation to engage in construction and achieve the goal of coexistence and co-prosperity. Therefore, we citizens recognize that Chinese directors can represent the public opinion of our citizens and implement the spirit of cooperation between China and foreign countries. Now, the Annual Meeting of Foreign Taxpayers has been moved by the erroneous and arrogant remarks of Mr. Mack to reject this minimum participation in municipal power. Who has given this kind of power and on what legal basis is it based? Moreover, the directors who manage municipal affairs have the same powers and status. Why is there so much emphasis on them and so little on us? Moreover, we have never heard of the election of Western directors being approved by the Chinese Taxpayers Association. Why should Chinese directors be approved by the Western Taxpayers Association? This is unfair. We, the Chinese people in the National Goods industry in Shanghai, solemnly declare that we do not recognize that foreigners have this power. All of us Chinese people are willing to fully cooperate with legitimate municipal organs and fulfill our tax obligations according to law. We pledge not to recognize any municipal or illegal organs that are not commensurate with them and await the resolution of our authorities. We hereby issue this declaration. Wang Jiean, Wang Xingyi, and Wang Hanqiang, the standing committee members of the China National Goods Maintenance Association, and all members jointly declare."

Public Works Bureau Calls Special Meeting 129

▲Yesterday a notice was issued.

▲Mr. Fessenden's Opinion

Sixty-one foreigners in this city jointly petitioned the senior consul on the 20th of this month to authorize the Public Works Bureau to convene a special meeting of Western ratepayers in the Public Concession at 5:30 PM on May 2nd to consider and pass the following motion proposed by Mr. Marshall and seconded by Mr. Baker: "Authorize and order the Public Works Bureau to propose to the countries concerned that the number of Chinese directors on the Public Works Bureau be increased from three to five." After receiving this petition, Senior Consul Cunningham convened a meeting of the consular body at his office on the evening of the 21st. After unanimous agreement, he notified the Public Works Bureau, which issued a notice yesterday convening the special meeting.

Mr. Fessenden, Director-General of the Public Works Bureau, expressed his opinion yesterday regarding the proposal to increase the number of Chinese directors on the Public Works Bureau, which will be considered at a special meeting of Western ratepayers. He said, "I believe this proposal will be enthusiastically supported by those present. To my knowledge, none of the directors of the Public Works Bureau do not welcome this proposal, so I expect public opinion will also support it. The passage of this proposal is very certain."

Upriver Foreign Vessels Resume Service After More Than a Month's Strike 130

▲Labor disputes in Yichang and Chongqing have been resolved.

▲Labor dispute in upstream area to be resolved. Since the employees on the upstream of Yangtze River, from Yichang to Chongqing, requested a pay raise and were rejected by British and Japanese foreign vessels, the vessels automatically suspended service to resist. Both sides went to extremes, and the foreign vessels between Yichang and Chongqing had been suspended for a month. Recently, the Chongqing Shipping Association, etc., pointed out that the long-term strike caused by the pay raise would not only affect transportation, but also cause significant losses to both labor and capital. Therefore, they acted as mediators to persuade both sides to compromise and resolve the issue as soon as possible. Yesterday, this city received a telegram from Yichang stating that British and Japanese shipping companies have accepted the request from upstream workers, and the amount of the pay raise is under negotiation. Therefore, the British and Japanese foreign vessels that suspended business in Shanghai have decided to order the Qinghe, Fuhe, and other ships to set sail for resumption of service starting from the 25th.

▲Loading and unloading wages may be appropriately increased. The Yichang Stevedores' Union requested a doubling of wages, which was rejected by the shipowners, leading to a strike. At that time, the Yichang Shipping Association intervened and advised that when the upstream foreign vessels were suspended and Chinese ships were operating, the overall situation should be taken into consideration. The workers then continued to work as usual. However, regarding the wage increase, the Yichang Shipping Association and the Stevedores' Union jointly sent representatives to Shanghai to discuss with the shipowners. It is reported that after several days of meetings, the shipping companies have agreed to change the original wage of 150 cash per piece to 5 cents per piece. Since the exchange rate in Yichang is 4,000 cash per silver dollar, this is an increase of one-third. A peaceful resolution of this issue is expected.

▲The Emei Wheel is temporarily difficult to operate. After major repairs in Shanghai, the China Merchants Bureau's upstream vessel Emei was originally scheduled to go to Chongqing when foreign merchant ships suspended service. Therefore, the repairs were completed, and it was planning to transport goods to Chongqing. However, it recently received a telegram from the Ministry of Communications stating that it was needed and instructed to postpone the opening of commercial routes. In a day or two, the ship will have to sail to Nanjing. In addition, the Chang'an and Dexing vessels of Sanbei received telegrams from Hankou stating that it would be difficult to resume service for a while.

▲Ning Shao New Wheel Plans to Rent. The Norwegian wheel purchased by Ning Shao Company for 14,000 pounds was originally intended to expand the Yangtze River shipping industry. Now the wheel has been renamed Ning Jing. Yesterday, it was reported to the Jianghai Customs to change the Chinese flag. Recently, due to the shortage of commercial goods on the Yangtze River, the company has decided not to send the ship to the Shanghai-Hankou route for the time being. It is planning to rent it out first, switch to sea routes, and then take it back for its own use after the situation is slightly calmer, and join the Yangtze River route.

Continued News of Rice Price Stabilization Committee 131

▲Starting from May 1st

The Municipal Rice Price Stabilization Committee was established on the 16th of this month. Recently, it has been working tirelessly. Chairman Pan is supervising the procurement and public sales of affordable rice day and night, and the committee members are responsible for planning and implementing the work. It is also reported that the committee is scheduled to start handling affordable rice on May 1st. Yesterday, the first batch of more than 500 bags of foreign rice was obtained.

Business Reorganization Committee Raises Funds for Rice Price Stabilization Losses 132

The Business Reorganization Committee believes that the rice price in this city has soared, reaching more than 21 yuan per stone. As the period between the harvest seasons is approaching, the hidden dangers are worrisome if precautions are not taken early. Previously, the Municipal Food Committee decided to purchase 200,000 bags of foreign rice in succession to handle affordable rice. However, the funds for the losses have not been settled. Now the Social Affairs Bureau plans to raise 100,000 to 150,000 yuan to compensate. In addition to the allocations from various groups, municipal governments, silver industry, and rice industry, there is still a shortage of 30,000 yuan. It is reported that the Business Reorganization Committee has sent letters to its affiliated industry groups yesterday, setting a joint meeting at 2:00 PM on the 24th of this month to discuss fundraising methods so that affordable rice can be sold early to feed the people.

Party and Government Circles Advocate Thrift Movement 133

The Shanghai Special Municipal Government yesterday approved a letter from the Shanghai Special Municipal Executive Committee of the Chinese Nationalist Party, stating: "According to a report from the Fourth District Party Department of the Association, the economic situation in our country is extremely difficult. On the one hand, it is subject to the oppression of imperialist financial capitalism, and on the other hand, it is due to the people's pursuit of luxury and lack of production. Since Mr. He Yingqin initiated the thrift movement, he has called for a high level of response. Although it is a passive movement, after saving, there will be more financial investment. Consumption is used passively to achieve active purposes. National economy and people's livelihood depend on it for more benefits. Party members and civil servants should especially take the lead in setting an example to serve as a model. Therefore, we specially request the council to order all party members in the city to pay close attention and also instruct the municipal government to instruct public and commercial personnel to abide by it in order to enrich the people's livelihood. According to this, the thrift movement is indeed enriching the country and enriching the people. Party members and civil servants are models for the people and should set an example and implement it in practice. According to the previous report, in addition to ordering all district party departments to strictly abide by it, we should also send a letter to your government for reference and hope that you will instruct your subordinates to pay close attention to it." Mayor Zhang has already instructed the affiliated public security, social education, public works, public utilities, finance, and health bureaus to refer to it together.

Signing of Sino-Japanese Tariff Treaty Still Pending 134

▲Shigemitsu will go to Beijing next month.

Guowen News Agency said, "It has been widely rumored that the Sino-Japanese tariff treaty has been formally approved by the Japanese government, and that Chargé d'Affaires Shigemitsu will go to Beijing to sign it within days. In fact, these are all speculations. According to news from the Japanese embassy office yesterday, although this draft Sino-Japanese tariff treaty has been passed by the Japanese Privy Council twice, according to procedures, it must still be submitted back to the Japanese cabinet meeting for formal discussion and approval, and it must be submitted to the Japanese Emperor for approval before the Chargé d'Affaires can be instructed to sign it. It is now heard that the Japanese cabinet has scheduled a cabinet meeting around the 30th of this month to discuss this matter, and Japanese Chargé d'Affaires Shigemitsu Kui has been busy preparing for the celebration of the Emperor's birthday in Shanghai for days. On the 29th, the Emperor's birthday, he must host Chinese and foreign guests in Shanghai and preside over the meeting. He really has no time to go to Beijing. Therefore, the official signing date must be at the beginning of next month at the earliest. Chargé d'Affaires Shigemitsu has also scheduled to go to Beijing on the morning or evening of the 2nd of next month."
