Liu Jiwen Scheduled to be Sworn in 137

▲On the 25th of this month

The newly appointed Superintendent of Jianghai Customs, Liu Jiwen, arrived at the office the day before yesterday and assumed his new post, as reported in yesterday's newspaper. It is now learned that Liu has selected a date to hold the swearing-in ceremony and has appointed various officials in the office. The following are the various news items:

▲Scheduled to be Sworn in. Liu has selected the 25th of this month to hold the swearing-in ceremony at the Superintendent of Customs Office on Xinzha Road. Yesterday morning, he sent telegrams to the National Government, the Executive Yuan, and the Ministry of Finance, requesting them to send officials to Shanghai to supervise the swearing-in ceremony.

▲Appointing New and Old Officials. The office originally had four sections. After handling the handover with the old office the day before yesterday, Liu ordered Liu Mengchun to take over the General Affairs Section, Yu Xijiu to take over the Accounting Section, and Xu Tigang to take over the Taxation Section, all of whom were responsible for the section chief. However, the official order has not yet been issued. The former Chief of the Taxation Section, Shen Qiyu, was transferred to Chief of the Navigation Administration Section, and Zhang Xifan was appointed as Secretary. The former Secretary, Wang Jingshun, was reassigned as a Tax Liaison Officer. Long Gongying collected the seals. The accounting of Jiao Wu was newly appointed. The remaining old officials were all additionally appointed yesterday morning. The office originally had a chief accountant, who was directly appointed by the Ministry of Finance. He has not yet arrived.

▲To Meet with Tax Commissioner Tomorrow. Liu is scheduled to visit Tax Commissioner Meyer and Jianghai Customs Tax Commissioner Mei Weiliang tomorrow (the 24th) to discuss everything. The notice was issued yesterday.

▲Scheduled to Visit Various Consuls. Liu also believes that taxation is related to various countries and plans to visit or meet with consuls of various countries regularly. Yesterday, he instructed Tax Liaison Officer Wang Jingshun to contact the consulates of various countries to arrange a meeting.

Naval Freshmen Arrived in Port Yesterday Afternoon 138

▲Because of rushing to make student uniforms

▲Staying in Shanghai for three or four days

The naval Jing'an transport ship, which carried 96 naval freshmen from Beijing the day before yesterday to study at the Fuzhou Naval Academy, sailed in from Wusongkou yesterday afternoon and arrived at the Nanjing Gaochang Temple Wharf at 1:00 p.m., moored in the Huangpu River. A reporter from the Daily News visited the ship yesterday to see the students and hear about the examination process from Captain Ouyang Ji. Details are as follows:

▲Examination Process. The naval freshmen who passed the examination this time were recommended by the provincial governments. Before being sent to the Ministry of the Navy, the education authorities of each province and city conducted an examination first. Those who were admitted were all graduates of higher primary schools or above. After passing the examination, they were sent to the Ministry of the Navy for examination. A total of more than 160 people were sent from various provinces and cities. Among them, more than 40 people were not admitted due to physical examination and slightly inferior eyesight, which is a pity. Only 97 people were strictly admitted by the Examination Committee. When they were led on board the ship the day before yesterday, one student had a temporary problem, so 96 students were sent to study.

▲Student Age. The youngest student is 12 years old, accounting for half of the team. The oldest is only 15 years old. The students are all energetic and have no homesickness. It is commendable.

▲Rushing to Make Military Uniforms. Yesterday afternoon, after the ship arrived in port, the naval management office in this port ordered the new clothing store to rush to make student uniforms and leather shoes. The color of the uniforms is evergreen serge and black leather shoes. The uniforms must be rushed overnight and will be made this afternoon to distribute to the students. The casual clothes that are changed will be kept or sent to the students' homes.

▲Family Visits. Yesterday afternoon around 2:00 p.m., a small number of students' family elders went to the ship to visit and express their cordial greetings. The adjutant of the ship received them, which was very satisfactory to the parents. ▲Leading to See Shipyard. Yesterday, the students were not taken to visit the shipyard and various factories because the uniforms had not yet been made. After the uniforms are distributed, the captain of the ship will lead them ashore to visit the factories.

▲Graduation Deadline. After being admitted, the students will enter the school as recruits for six months, and then formally attend classes. Graduation from the school is five years, and then practice on the engine for one year, navigation for one year, and placement of artillery positions for one year, for a total of eight years. Only then can they be considered officially graduated. The best ones will be sent to Europe and the United States to study. However, during these eight years, they may not ask for leave to go home for no reason. There is no vacation or holiday in the school.

▲Departure Date. The ship was originally scheduled to stay in Shanghai for a short time after arriving. However, because the student uniforms are custom-made in Shanghai, it will not be possible to catch up in three days. Therefore, the ship will stay for about three or four days.

Regulations of the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau for Handling Labor Disputes 139

The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, in view of the importance of handling labor disputes, and taking advantage of the promulgation of the new law, has specially revised the internal handling procedures with reference to past practices and formulated the Regulations for Handling Labor Disputes, which consist of 11 articles, to show the standard. The regulations have been submitted to the Municipal Government for approval and record. The articles are recorded as follows: Article 1. These Regulations are established to regulate the general procedures for the Bureau to handle labor disputes. Those with special circumstances and specially approved by the Director shall not be subject to this restriction. Article 2. After receiving the mediation application or petition from the disputing parties, the Bureau shall designate the handling personnel by the Director or the Chief of the Competent Section to first examine the reasons for the application and assign them to the following categories: (A) If the reasons for the application are obviously illegal, or the request for correction is due to the other party's obviously illegal actions, or the matter obviously falls within the scope of the judiciary, after clarifying the investigation, the Chief of the Section shall submit a memorandum to the Director for approval, and the Writing Section shall draft a reply to be issued. (B) If the dispute cannot be handled by the Labor Dispute Resolution Law to organize a mediation committee, the Chief of the Section shall submit a memorandum and send personnel to handle it. (C) If the dispute can be handled by the Labor Dispute Resolution Law, the Chief of the Section shall submit a memorandum to the Director to convene a mediation committee for mediation and designate the Chairman of the Committee. Article 3. If the handling personnel have any questions about the reasons stated in the mediation application, they may summon the parties concerned to the Bureau for inquiry. Article 4. If a party applies for mediation due to a dispute, the mediation application shall be the legal document. The Bureau's acceptance of handling labor disputes shall also be based solely on the mediation application. The aforementioned mediation application shall be prepared in two copies, original and duplicate. The Bureau shall formulate the format in accordance with the provisions of Article 20 of the Labor Dispute Resolution Law, and the parties concerned shall fill it out in the prescribed format. If they do not comply, they shall be regarded as non-compliant with the format and may not be accepted. However, if the parties' petition has included all the items that should be recorded in the mediation application, the Bureau may fill out the mediation application on their behalf and attach the original petition. Article 5. When the handling of Article 2, Item B of these Regulations is completed, the handling personnel shall submit the handling results together with the relevant documents to the Director or report to the Director. Article 6. The Chairman of the Mediation Committee shall report the mediation process together with all the documents of the case for record in accordance with Article 2, Item C of these Regulations. Article 7. If the aforementioned mediation is successful, the Mediation Committee shall send the original draft of the mediation record to the Director for review, then print the original copy and send it directly to the parties concerned. In addition, the Bureau shall instruct both parties to comply with the implementation. If it is not successful, the Bureau shall inform both parties and restrict the parties' actions when necessary. Article 8. All cases that are issued for handling or mediation shall be compiled into a file in accordance with the order of all the documents of the case by the handling personnel upon completion. Article 9. If the Mediation Committee wants to request the Bureau to issue a document to a third party due to an accident, it shall submit a written request for examination. Article 10. When investigators and clerks of the Bureau handle mediation matters, they shall regard the Chairman of the Mediation Committee as their immediate superior for reporting on the matters they are handling. Article 11. These Regulations shall be implemented from the date of approval and record by the Special Municipal Government.

Unemployed Workers of Nanyang Tobacco Factory Appeal to All Circles for Assistance 140

The National Society stated that the delegation of unemployed workers of the Nanyang Tobacco Company in this city issued a declaration yesterday, saying: "The Central Committee of the Chinese Nationalist Party, the President and Ministers of various courts and ministries of the National Government, various agencies, various newspapers, and various trade unions are all aware that since the Nanyang Tobacco Company suddenly announced at the end of the lunar year that the Shanghai factory would be closed, the company claimed that the reason for the closure was that the cost was huge, the price of gold soared, and the tariffs were too heavy, so it had to be closed. However, in reality, it had ulterior motives. Last year, it used workers' disputes, such as bribing the reorganization committee, organizing the Labor-Capital Cooperation Committee, and abolishing the trade union founded by Sun Yat-sen. All of the above provoked workers to fight each other in order to achieve its oppression and slaughter doctrine. However, people from all walks of life are still in the dark about this situation. Now, let us reiterate that after the eighth executive committee of the trade union had a dispute in May last year, the superior party department believed that its organization was poor and had to be rectified, so the reorganization committee was created. At that time, a few bad worker traitors colluded with the capitalist representative Li Hun and others in the name of reorganization. As a result, more than 200 good workers were expelled. In November, the capitalist suddenly instigated the reorganization committee to believe that the reactionary eighth executive committee of the trade union had returned to the factory, and the capitalist organized the so-called Labor-Capital Cooperation Committee, forcibly taking over all the documents of the reorganization committee, and shouting to overthrow the reorganization committee, automatically canceling the trade union, overturning the original preferential conditions for workers, and formulating a labor-capital cooperation treaty. At the same time, the capitalist bribed bad workers, and the capitalist came forward to hold a puppet congress, forcibly implementing it. Xie Li Jianfudeng also gave a speech on the stage, patting his chest and swearing that he would never fire workers at the end of the year in order to bait the workers not to oppose it. Who knows that the notice of not firing workers was not yet dry, and the closure of the factory has been seen, going back on its word and announcing a complete closure, disregarding the lives of thousands of workers. All kinds of vicious methods are aimed at making our thousands of workers starve to death as soon as possible. Moreover, this closure has not been approved by the government, and there was no indication before the deadline. They do not know that there is a party, a country, a nation, or laws. The government has promulgated the Limited Company and Factory Regulations. Companies and factories must lose more than half of their capital before they can declare bankruptcy or apply for government assistance. Only if the government cannot maintain it can it be approved to close the factory. The capital of the Nanyang Tobacco Company is 15 million yuan, and the surplus public reserve in the 14th and 15th years of the Republic of China reached more than 4 million yuan. Then, together with the original capital, the exact number is 20 million yuan. Although the 16th, 17th, and 18th years of the Republic of China reported losses, they have not yet gone bankrupt. They have only lost the public reserve, and the original assets are still intact. Therefore, the closure of the Shanghai factory is not for this reason. Moreover, the tax in Hong Kong is heavier than that in the Shanghai factory, but the Hong Kong factory is still working day and night to manufacture. Then, the reason why the company closed the Shanghai factory is not only because the price of gold and the tax rate have increased. Recently, various newspapers suddenly claimed that the Nanyang Company was operating as usual. It is expected that all circles have also understood. According to the company's statement, the factory costs are too high and the production volume is too far apart, so it has to temporarily suspend operations for reorganization. As for the collection of goods in various places, it is temporarily supplied by Hong Kong manufacturing. In reality, it entrusts San You, Zhongyuan, Xinmin and other tobacco factories to manufacture. Moreover, its announcement in Beijing claims that the collection of goods in various places has increased rather than decreased. It entrusts other factories to manufacture tobacco, falsely claiming that it is manufactured in the Hong Kong factory. All kinds of deceptive means show that the closure of the Nanyang Company is not as thorough as its declaration, and the reasons for the closure are not sufficient. The purpose is to use this as an excuse to oppress the workers. At this time when the political training has begun, the interests of the workers are carefully maintained by the late General and the orders of the government cannot allow the capitalists to freely slaughter the workers. Under the banner of the blue sky and white sun, such a major problem has occurred. People from all walks of life have been silent and speak out for our Nanyang workers, so that our thousands of workers are immersed in the sea of suffering and oppressed under the iron hoof of the capitalists. We hope that people from all walks of life will speak out for our Nanyang workers and ask the competent authorities at all levels to limit the Nanyang Tobacco Company to open the factory immediately to relieve the suffering of unemployed workers, and to negotiate with the factory on behalf of the representatives, even if they sacrifice everything, they will not hesitate to lead all the workers to resist the vicious capitalists and their lackeys in order to achieve our late General's policy of supporting the workers, and to ask the superiors to stop various tobacco factories from manufacturing tobacco for Nanyang to maintain the livelihoods of the workers. We hereby declare our slogans: (1) We want all party and government agencies to quickly order Nanyang to open the factory and resume work. (2) Overthrow the worker traitors such as Li Hui, who plotted for personal gain, auctioned off the workers, and caused this closure. (3) Ask the superior party department to stop various tobacco factories from manufacturing tobacco for Nanyang. (4) Workers, unite. (5) Long live the Chinese Nationalist Party! The Nanyang Tobacco Factory All Workers Unemployment Delegation, respectfully.

Record of the Continued General Meeting of the Red Cross Society 144

The Chinese Red Cross Society continued its meeting yesterday at 10:00 AM. There were 128 representatives from branch offices and 60 members present. The chairmen were Li Cishan, Jiang Daqiu, Wang Peiyuan, and Wen Lanting. Ji Heqin and Wei Ruifeng served as recorders. The proceedings began as usual. First, Dong Lin, the representative from the Luxian branch, and Wu Jiasan, the representative from the Shexian branch, and others, proposed a temporary motion to change the agenda. They suggested that after the proposals were discussed thoroughly and the representatives fully understood the content, philanthropists and individuals with reputation and responsibility should be elected. They also emphasized the need to increase the number of branch representatives to develop the society's affairs. Zhang Tianxi opposed this proposal. The chairman put it to a vote, and the majority voted in favor of the change, so it passed. Niu Bingjun, the representative from Dongtai, proposed a regulation on voting rights, setting the standard as 30 rights for each representative and one right for each member. This was also passed. The representative from the Gaozi branch moved that the head office nursing school should have each branch recommend students in accordance with the regulations. Chairman Wang Peiyuan described the establishment of the nursing school. Of the 60 students, 40 would be recommended by the branches and 20 would be recruited through examinations in Shanghai. There were no objections, and the motion was passed. Jiang Daqiu, the representative from the Huai'an branch, proposed that all income and expenditure related to the Red Cross's disaster relief efforts should be publicly announced in the newspapers. Regarding the distribution procedures, the identity of the organizations involved, the roster of affected people, and the distribution voucher stubs should all be kept on file for review. Everyone agreed, and the motion was passed. Yue Bingjun, the representative from Dongtai, proposed that the Red Cross should have a permanent memorial day to expand its operations, specifically designating July 8, 1904, the date the Red Cross officially joined the International Alliance, as the permanent memorial day. This was passed. The meeting adjourned at 12:00 PM. At 2:00 PM, the meeting resumed to discuss proposals: (1) The Cangxian branch proposed a ban on armed fundraising and fraud. Ji Heqin, the representative from Lianshui, supplemented the reasons, and the motion was passed. (2) The Jiashan Xitang branch proposed that ordinary members should have the right to be elected and propose motions, but because it conflicted with the regulations, it was not adopted. (3) The proposal that student members should be given full rights was explained by Ji Heqin, the representative from Lianshui, and it was passed. (4) The proposal that the Society should stipulate a period for carrying out certain charitable activities was referred to the Standing Committee for approval. (5) The representative from the Wuzhou branch proposed that in the event of wartime use of aircraft and the dropping of bombs, causing damage to civilian houses, the military commanders on both sides should carefully investigate, which was referred to the Standing Committee for approval. (6) If branches go to various places to raise funds, the head office should first send a letter to the local branch or local government for notification before arriving to raise funds, but this does not apply to voluntary donations from abroad. The motion was passed. (7) The Chu Wang branch proposed that the government should order officials in all provinces to assist in handling cases, and requested that the government, along with military and civilian leaders of all provinces, earnestly protect the members, which was referred to the Executive Committee and passed. (8) The proposal to reform the society's uniforms was referred to the Executive Committee for prompt handling and passed.

Local News 2

Sino-Italian Airline Opens Unprecedented Fast Ship 148

▲ Can Reach Europe in 24 Days

▲ Major Changes Will Occur in Sino-European Shipping

▲ Breaking the Record of Sino-European Sea Voyage

The fierce competition in the shipping industry in recent years can be described as reaching its peak. Pacific US-Japan shipping companies took the lead, followed by the New York route, each investing huge capital to build fast ships. Shortening the sea voyage would give them a business advantage. On the Sino-European route, after the British company built a 16,000-ton giant ship last year, shortening the journey from Shanghai to London from 45 days to 39 days, today Blue Funnel Line and Nippon Yusen, etc., are also building strong fast ships to compete. The Italian shipping company has added two unprecedentedly fast mail ships to the Sino-Italian line for future service in Shanghai. Once opened, the Sino-European route can be shortened by more than ten days. After the news spread, a major change will occur in the European shipping industry in Shanghai. The details are as follows:

▲ Expansion of Sino-Italian Line: The Italian postal shipping company, originally named LeoydTriestino, specializes in the Sino-Italian line with four existing postal ships and four cargo ships, each running once a month. Recently, the largest shipping company in Italy, named CisulichLine, has joined the company and is implementing a large-scale expansion of its shipping business in China in the Far East. It will start with passenger ships in order to gain a superior position on the Sino-European route. Therefore, it decided to add two of the largest passenger ships.

▲ Two Giant Ships Added First: The Italian post office in Shanghai has received a telegram from its home country stating that two large mail ships with a net tonnage of 24,000 tons each are being prepared to be sent to China for service, one named Saturnia and the other named Vuecania. Each ship is 631 feet long, 79 feet 6 inches wide, and 91 feet 11 inches high, divided into seven levels from top to bottom. There are 420 first-class rooms inside, including a smoking room, dance hall, swimming pool, glass garden, gymnasium, library, social hall, etc. The beauty of its setting and the size of the ship are unparalleled in the Sino-European route today, making it the largest ship.

▲ Arrive in Europe in 24 Days: The fastest mail ship from Shanghai to Europe (regardless of Britain, France, Italy, or Germany) takes at least 36-37 days, and ordinary ships take more than 40 days. Even the company's current three mail ships, such as the Aeskui, take 45 days to reach Italy. Now, the two newly added giant ships, powered by a motor engine, have an engine with 33,000 horsepower each, and the speed per hour exceeds 20 nautical miles. Therefore, it only takes 24 days to reach Trieste in Italy from Shanghai, reducing the sea voyage by 21 days compared to the current ships. This speed of mail ship is the first of its kind in the Far East.

▲ New Ships Will Come to Shanghai: The ship design drawings of the two ships have been sent to Shanghai. They are expected to arrive in Shanghai in about two months. Therefore, the company has received an order from its headquarters to stop selling tickets for the current three mail ships starting in June in order to wait for the two new ships to arrive and continue the three fast ships on schedule. It is heard that the two ships will only carry passengers and mail and will not load any cargo.

Zhuang Xueqing Commits Suicide Due to Family Pressure 149

▲ Stepmother Loves Her Young Daughter

▲ Years of Litigation Over Land Disputes

▲ Also Accused of Civil and Criminal Cases

▲ Zhuang Xueqing Resentfully Committed Suicide

Zhuang Xueqing, a local from Xiaoshiqiaotou, Pudong, committed suicide by swallowing opium yesterday afternoon due to resentment over losing a land dispute with his aunt. The situation is very complicated. The details are as follows:

▲ Family Situation of the Deceased: The deceased, Zhuang Xueqing, was 29 years old, a native of Pudong, who used to live at No. 12, Xiaoyangjing Miaodong, Xiaoshiqiaotou, Pudong. He used to be a copper smith on the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway, but he is now unemployed. His wife, Yang, is 28 years old and has a four-year-old son. Xueqing has four brothers: the eldest, Zhusheng; the second, Zhulin; Xueqing is the third; and the fourth, Zhufa. All are married.

▲ Adopted by Aunt as Son: Xueqing had an uncle, Jinsheng, who died of illness in 1917, leaving his wife, Zhang (Xueqing's aunt), who is now 44 years old. She had two daughters. At that time, because Zhang had no son to inherit the family line, the relatives persuaded Xueqing to be adopted as her son to inherit the property, which was about ten mu of land, including a five-room house (the base of Zhuang's residence). The land deed was managed by Xueqing himself.

▲ Years of Litigation Over Land Disputes: Later, Zhang's eldest daughter married, and her second daughter, Zhang Bao (now 17 years old), was also engaged to the son of a Xu family nearby. Zhang loved Zhang Bao very much and said that she would live with Zhang Bao in the future. Therefore, she changed her attitude towards her adopted son Xueqing, treating him like a thorn in her side and was unwilling to leave the property under Xueqing's control. Therefore, she gradually sold almost all of it. All that remained was one and three-tenths of a mu of homestead land and five rooms of houses in Xueqing's hands. Zhang was still not satisfied and went to court to demand the return of the land deed for the one and three-tenths of a mu of homestead land, resulting in years of litigation with Xueqing that remained unresolved.

▲ Dissatisfaction with Sister's Freedom: After Zhang's second daughter, Zhang Bao, was engaged to the Xu family, the two sides often interacted to show their affection. However, Xueqing believed that an unmarried woman should not often live in her future husband's house. Therefore, last year, he took Zhang Bao home. The Xu family found out and reported to the police, who arrested Xueqing and Zhang Bao and sent them to the Third District Police Station. The district chief ruled that it was a marriage dispute and refused to intervene, deepening the feud.

▲ Civil and Criminal Cases Came One After Another: Zhang was very angry that Xueqing interfered with her daughter's freedom and filed a criminal complaint in court, accusing him of violating the criminal law. Then, she filed a civil suit to recover the one and three-tenths of a mu of homestead land deed held by Xueqing. The land deed had been mortgaged by Xueqing to a friend for 500 yuan three years ago, and the principal and interest had not been repaid. Recently, the court repeatedly urged the return of the land deed. Xueqing had no choice but to borrow 800 yuan from relatives and friends to redeem the land deed and send it to the court for filing. At this point, Xueqing was overwhelmed by the successive criminal and civil cases, and his resentment reached its peak. ▲ Sister's Wedding Date: Xueqing Commits Suicide: Yesterday was the wedding date for Zhang's second daughter, Zhang Bao. Xueqing, seeing that the land deed had been lost and that there was no hope of recovering it, was filled with resentment and had nowhere to vent it. He became extremely angry and suddenly had the idea of committing suicide. He secretly wrote four suicide notes. At 3:00 PM, while his wife was returning to her mother's house, he suddenly swallowed opium. When his wife returned from her mother's house, only ten minutes later, she saw Xueqing lying on the bed, his face ashen. When he saw his wife arrive, he got up and held Yang's hand, but when he wanted to say something to comfort her, he was already poisoned and unable to speak. Yang was frightened and immediately sent someone to Pudong Hospital to ask a doctor to come to the house for treatment. By the time he arrived, he had already died and could not be saved. Yang hugged her husband's body and cried loudly. She then reported to the Third District Police Station and asked the local security officer to request an autopsy from the local court.

▲ Summary of the Suicide Note: After Xueqing's death, his wife, Yang, found four suicide notes he had left. The key points are summarized below: (Letter to Relatives and Friends): "Because Zhuang Zhang, as (should be a mistake) my aunt, in 1917, my uncle died of illness. But Xue was working in the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway, and my aunt personally asked Lu Yinsheng and others to persuade me to take over the position of adopted son. I have been managing the funeral for thirteen years. I did not expect that after twelve years, my aunt would file a lawsuit to return the land deed, which has not been resolved to this day. Recently, successive civil and criminal lawsuits have come one after another, but my heart is broken, so I commit suicide and go to the West to declare that this kind of behavior is extremely sinful, my heart aches, it's injustice, it's wronged." (Farewell Letter to Wife): "My dear wife, this is a goodbye, but (only a mistake) I blame my own bad luck. In recent years, business has been very good, but I have encountered this kind of lawsuit, and I am sad and anxious, unable to sleep day and night, so (only a mistake) I can only commit suicide. You will not have enjoyment in this life, but I will repay you in the next life as an ox or a horse. Goodbye." There are two more letters, which are not important, so they are omitted.

Woman Trafficker's Family Ruined 150

▲ Tragic Situation After Yao Wang's Conviction

▲ Father Drowned Himself, Three Houses Demolished

Yao Wang, a woman from Suzhou, took young girls Zhu Xingnv, Lu Jinxiu, etc. on the Taikoo Company's Tongzhou ship from Shanghai last month, intending to go to Tianjin. When the ship was about to depart, detectives from the Women and Children Relief Society checked the ship and found them suspicious. They detained the girls Chen Yueying, etc., along with their luggage, and sent them to the Shanghai Local Court Prosecutor's Office. After investigation, Yao Wang was sentenced to one year and four months in prison, and Chen Yueying was acquitted and released on bail. The two young girls, Zhu and Lu, were sent to the Women and Children Relief Society's orphanage. After Yao Wang received the verdict, she lacked the ability to appeal and had to abandon the appeal and voluntarily serve her sentence. However, Yao Wang's family had a 66-year-old father living in the countryside in Suzhou, who relied on his daughter for support. Upon receiving the news of the verdict, he drowned himself two weeks ago. At that time, relatives and friends hastily put Wang's father in a coffin and buried it in the field. Unexpectedly, a neighbor's family had a sudden illness and died, and because they suspected that the coffin was placed on the seven killers' head, they gathered many people and demolished the three houses of the person who drowned himself, leaving nothing. Yao Wang, although in custody, has been there for a total of six weeks. After her relatives notified her, she had no choice but to accept it. Although Chen Yueying was acquitted and released, the three suitcases and bedding that were detained, as well as the two young girls, Zhu and Lu, who were detained in the orphanage as victims, also became ill after being sent to the orphanage. The families have been submitting requests to the Shanghai Local Court Prosecutor's Office for the return of their loved ones. The Local Court Prosecutor's Office will issue a release order as soon as the case file is returned.

Record of the Higher Branch Court's Interrogation of the Blind Man's Brutality Yesterday 153

▲ Blind Man Violently Assaulted an Eleven-Year-Old Girl

▲ Refuses to Accept Eight-Year Prison Sentence

▲ How Could He Rape If He Was Not in Shanghai?

▲ The Period When the Blind Man Was in Shanghai Is Worth Studying

Shan Huaibao, a 19-year-old man from Jiangbei, lost his eyesight at an early age. His family made him learn the art of fortune-telling to make a living. Shan lived at No. 264 Ruijin Road. Jiang Wu, a woman who lived in the same house, had an 11-year-old daughter, Wendi. At 6:00 PM on November 6th last year, Shan raped her. Afterwards, the woman filed a complaint, and the former Provisional Court sentenced Shan to eight years in prison. Shan still refused to accept this and filed an appeal. Yesterday afternoon, the Higher Branch Court opened the trial, attended by Judge Song Yuan, Judge Du Fuyue, Ye Zaizhou, and Chief Prosecutor Wang Zhennan. First, the appellant, Shan Huaibao, claimed, "Jiang Wu accused me of raping her young daughter. If it is a fact, I am willing to be punished, but I returned to my hometown from September 11th last year until I returned to Shanghai on December 23rd. On the day she accused me of raping her, I had not yet come to Shanghai, so how could I rape her? Jiang Wu lived in the front of the attic on the third floor of the house, and I lived in the back. Therefore, her mother and daughter had to pass through my room to enter the room. I also asked Wendi to buy things from time to time. All the clothes were washed by her. Once, I had a quarrel because the clothes she washed were missing, and I kicked her, which may have caused her to hate me and falsely accuse me. Moreover, she accused me of raping her on the 6th of the month, so why did she not report it to the police station until the 9th? I ask for a clear investigation." Then, according to Jiang Wu, "At 6:00 PM on November 6th last year, I was cooking when I saw Shan hurriedly descending from the attic on the third floor. I was very suspicious, so I went upstairs and saw my daughter groaning in the room. I asked her and learned that she had been bullied by Shan. According to my daughter, Shan forcibly pulled down her pants and raped her. Because Shan covered her mouth with one hand at the time, she could not shout. However, Shan knew that he had done wrong, so he fled. At first, I did not intend to publicize it, so I did not report it to the police station on that day. It was not until the 9th that Yue Li, a woman who lived in the kitchen of the house, gave me a dollar, saying that Shan's father had asked her to give it to Wendi to treat her injuries. I refused to accept it. Unexpectedly, Shan's father took the opportunity to ask me for his son, saying that his son Huaibao was missing and had been beaten to death by me. I had no choice but to send my daughter to Guangren Hospital to verify the rape injuries before filing a complaint." Also, according to the girl Jiang Wendi, "At that time, Shan called me to his room and forcibly pulled down my pants and raped me. Because he covered my mouth with one hand, I could not make a sound." Yue Li, a witness, said, "Shan Huaibao returned to Jiangbei last year, but I don't remember the date. On November 9th, Shan's father asked me to give Jiang Wu a dollar, but I don't know what it was for because the language barrier prevented me from knowing." Then, Shan's lawyer and the police lawyer debated each other. Finally, Prosecutor Wang expressed his opinion, saying that the facts of this case have been investigated clearly, and I ask the judges to make a judgment according to the law. The judge then declared the debate in this case over and adjourned the court to set a date for sentencing. Shan Huaibao was still taken back to the police station for detention.

Minor Punishment for Building a Private Road 155

The Daily News reported that the Municipal Land Bureau found that Kangyi Foreign Firm near the stadium on Jungong Road had privately rented private land to build a private road without obtaining a license and reporting it for record. In addition to ordering the firm to stop construction, it had reported to the municipal government whether to submit it to the municipal affairs meeting to discuss the handling method. Yesterday, the bureau received instructions from the municipal government, stating, "We have received the report. It is inappropriate for the foreign firm to build a private road across the public canal without applying for a license beforehand. The bureau should investigate in detail. If there is any blockage of the throat of the embankment or damage to farmland, the foreign firm should be ordered to repair and rebuild the bridge. In addition, they should complete the relevant procedures and impose a fine of 50 yuan in accordance with Article 26 of the bureau's temporary construction regulations for starting construction without a license and applying for repairs to show minor punishment. However, there are no explicit provisions in the regulations for citizens requesting the construction of bridges, docks, and revetments for the construction of private roads. The bureau should revise these regulations into the Shanghai Special City Citizens' Regulations for Requesting the Construction of Bridges, Docks, Revetments, and Private Roads and submit them for approval."

Japanese Prisoner Escapes En Route 157

Wenhui Daily reports that a Japanese man named Kaneda, about 23 years old and a clockmaker by trade, was employed by a Japanese clock shop on Miller Road. He was arrested for stealing jewelry worth $5,600 from the shop and confessed to the theft. He also agreed to lead Japanese consulate police to pawnshops in the International Settlement to recover the stolen goods. Some items had already been retrieved. However, at 10:30 AM the other day, while at a pawnshop, Kaneda suddenly claimed to have a stomach ache. The escorting patrolman took him to the lavatory in Kunshan Garden and waited outside. After a long time without him emerging, the patrolman went inside to check, only to find he had already fled. The Japanese consulate and the Public Concession police have been notified to issue an arrest warrant. As of yesterday, he had not yet been captured.

Recent Developments in the Construction of the Zhabei Water and Electricity Company's Yin Xing New Power Plant 159

The Zhabei Water and Electricity Company has been constructing a new power plant near the Jian Song Bridge in Yin Xing, along the riverbank. Construction began over a year ago, and the project is exceptionally large. It is reported that the construction is nearing completion. Most of the major machinery, such as boilers, steam turbines, generators, transformers, and switchboards, have been installed and completed by the Chinese and foreign engineers of the plant. The plant anticipates that all electrical equipment was shipped from abroad to Shanghai long ago. To prevent unexpected events at startup, the plant recently purchased a large quantity of firewood worth more than a thousand yuan to burn and bake, and will conduct a trial run after the moisture soaked into the equipment is completely dissipated. The date of officially supplying current will not be far off.

Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce Investigates Customs of the Tobacco Industry 161

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce sent a letter to the Special District Local Court yesterday, stating, "Respectfully, we received a letter No. 1015 from the former Shanghai International Settlement Temporary Court, stating that in case No. 6323 in the General Section of the Court, several points regarding the investigation of tobacco industry customs should be investigated: (1) Whether traveling salesmen hired by tobacco leaf merchants receive commissions in addition to their monthly salaries, or whether those who receive commissions are not paid a separate salary; (2) Whether the commission received by traveling salesmen is calculated at 1% of the sales price; (3) Whether traveling salesmen who receive commissions are liable for compensation for bad debts they handle. Regarding the above points, which are pending resolution, we hereby request your association to inquire with the Tobacco Industry Association and promptly investigate and reply." The Chamber sent investigators from the Investigation Department to conduct detailed investigations at the Chinese Cigarette Factory Association and the Cigarette Industry Association tobacco firms. The investigation revealed three points: (1) Some tobacco leaf salesmen receive commissions in addition to their salaries, while others only receive commissions and do not receive a monthly salary; (2) The commission received by salesmen is calculated either by the barrel or by the percentage. Those calculated by the barrel are about US$2 to US$5 per barrel, and those calculated by the percentage range from 0.5% to 1.5% of the sales price; (3) This point is very important, and the methods of various tobacco leaf firms are very inconsistent. However, in most cases, a written or oral contract is concluded between the parties when hiring a salesman, and there is an undertaking of compensation (with full or partial compensation), or there is no undertaking of compensation. If the parties have not entered into a contract, the discovered facts must be used as a measure. For example, if the customer account released by the salesman is approved by the person in charge of the firm, then the salesman is naturally not responsible for the bad debt. If the customer account released is at the discretion of the salesman, or the salesman declares responsibility before the release, then the salesman should be responsible for compensation in the event of a bad debt. Therefore, there is no fixed custom on this point, and the facts must be weighed to make a decision standard. We are hereby sending a letter with the investigation to you. Please investigate and verify."

Expedite Freight Transport at McGinn Station 162

Freight transport at the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway's McGinn Road Station is extremely congested, with an estimated 6,000 tons accumulated, all awaiting urgent shipment to Hangzhou. The Rolling Stock Department is currently working to expedite freight transport and sent telegrams to all stations yesterday, instructing them to quickly send empty freight cars to McGinn Road Station for loading and special train transport to Hangzhou.

Attention to Trolley Passengers 164

▲Beware of Pickpockets

In recent days, in the Public Concession, since the public bus drivers went on strike and stopped running, the trolley businesses on all lines have suddenly become prosperous. In particular, the trolleybuses on all lines are very crowded. Although the company has added vehicles, it is still not enough. As a result, the passengers are densely packed. Therefore, general pickpockets took the unique opportunity to apply their skills. As a result, cases of theft among passengers are frequently heard. At around 5:00 PM yesterday, a Mr. Cheng, who lived on Avenue Joffre in the French Concession and owned a hardware business, boarded an Route 18 trolley at the Xin Zha Bridge and got off at the Great World. His wallet containing more than 30 yuan was stolen from his pocket. Also, at around 4:00 PM the day before yesterday, a Mr. Zhang, who lived on Avenue Edward VII, took a trolley from Caojiadu back to Shanghai and his documents in an envelope in his pocket were stolen en route. Fortunately, there was no money in it. It is hoped that passengers will pay extra attention.

Arrests Made in Open-Air Meeting Case Transferred 165

▲Li Longzhi First Transferred, Police Apologize

▲Remaining Five Handed Over to Public Security Bureau for Interrogation and Return

On the wasteland in front of the Sanxing Yarn Factory on Yangshupu Road, there was a gathering and meeting the other day. The police dispatched detectives to arrest six participants: He Qingxiang, Yao Guanghua, Li Longzhi, Chen, Chen Jiaxing, Yan Zhaotang, and Song Chaowei. Along with anti-government printed materials, they were escorted to the Higher Branch Court for interrogation and detention. This was reported in yesterday's newspaper. It has been learned that one of the arrested, Li Longzhi, claimed to be from Beiping. However, after a detailed investigation by the police, it was confirmed that Li was indeed a Korean. Previously, he had been arrested by Japanese authorities in Korea for anti-government activities. He escaped while under investigation and came to China by ship from the United States. After arriving in Shanghai, he joined the Communist organization in Shanghai. The day before yesterday, in the early morning, he and his accomplices participated in an open-air meeting in front of the yarn factory and were arrested by the police. Upon hearing the news, the Japanese Consulate in Shanghai, believing that Li was an important fugitive, specially sent police officers to the political department of the general police station the day before yesterday evening to take Li to the Japanese Consulate. Yesterday morning, the police only transferred the remaining five to the Second Branch of the Jiangsu Higher Court. Judge Ye Zaichou continued to preside over the preliminary hearing. The police lawyer, Ru Bao Yi, first stated that the Japanese Consulate had sent someone to take Li Longzhi, saying that since Li was a Korean, the Court had no jurisdiction over him and was therefore taken away. However, the Japanese Consulate sent someone to the police station to pick him up near dusk, so it was not possible to ask for instructions in advance. The police apologized deeply, but because of the time constraints, they hoped that the Court would understand. Then, a representative from the Municipal Public Security Bureau delivered an official document requesting that the remaining five be transferred to them. Judge Ye immediately interrogated each defendant and approved the transfer of He Qingxiang and the other four to the officer Nie Yaxi for interrogation. After the Public Security Bureau returns them, the Special District Court will schedule a hearing. Regarding Li Longzhi's part, the police were ordered to submit written evidence for record.

Zhang Xingcun Obtains Creditor's Rights in Automobile Pledge Lawsuit 169

▲American Feng Bank Withdraws Lawsuit

▲Zhang Sues Based on Comprador Contract

Cheng A'gen of the Feilong Automobile Company previously ordered a car and the American Feng Bank pledged the funds. However, they ignored the pledged funds, exceeding tens of thousands, and were sued by the bank. After a ruling by the former Temporary Court, one party refused to accept the ruling and filed an appeal with the Chinese and Foreign Civil Appeals Office of the former Diplomatic Affairs Department. At the end of last year, the Diplomatic Affairs Department was ordered to be abolished, and the attached Appeals Office ceased operations. The case was therefore not heard. However, the American Feng Bank's pledge was made by the comprador Zhang Xingcun. Now that Zhang has resigned, the bank believes that according to the comprador contract signed with Zhang, all funds handled by Zhang should be cleared upon resignation. Therefore, the funds owed by Cheng have already been compensated by Zhang, and Zhang has obtained the assignment of the creditor's rights. Zhang then hired lawyer Shen Yuesheng and filed a lawsuit with the Special District Local Court, requesting a judgment ordering the defendant Cheng A'gen to repay the funds paid on his behalf. Yesterday morning, Judge Ying Shi presided over the hearing. Lawyer Shen stated the details of the case and submitted several copies of the American Feng Bank's judgment against Cheng as evidence. The defendant Cheng A'gen did not appear, and lawyer Fan Gang appeared as his agent and argued that the case had already been appealed and should await the appellate court's judgment. Furthermore, the defendant's dispute was with the American Feng Bank, and it is incomprehensible that Mr. Zhang is now suing. Lawyer Shen then restated the course of events, saying that the appeal had been withdrawn, and that Zhang Xingcun had already compensated the funds according to the comprador contract and had notified the defendant after obtaining the right to assign the creditor's rights from the American Feng Bank, so Zhang had the right to sue. The presiding judge immediately instructed Lawyer Shen to submit evidence of notifying the defendant and detailed accounts for further investigation.

Bathhouse Owner Attempts Suicide 171

▲Befriending Bad People

▲Unable to Bear Oppression, He Planned To End It

The ferry at the Fenshan Wharf in Pudong loaded more than 20 passengers from Hongkou, Puxi, at 8:00 AM yesterday and sailed back to Pudong. Unexpectedly, as the boat reached the center of the river, a passenger, about 40 years old, walked out of the cabin and jumped into the river to commit suicide. Fortunately, the tide was calm at the time, and he immediately resurfaced. The boatman used a bamboo pole to hook him and rescue him from drowning. The boat then arrived at the Pudong wharf, and the passenger was handed over to the police of the Fourth Squadron, who transferred him to the Third District of the Public Security Bureau. He confessed that his name was Sun Xinqi, 44 years old, from Qingjiang. He lived at 21 Qianyi Lane, Hujia Muqiao, Hongkou. He owned the Jin Shuangquan Bathhouse in that area. The business was not bad, but later friends such as Yin Xinzhi joined as shareholders, and the business gradually declined, resulting in huge losses. Now Yin and others plan to sell the bathhouse, but I did not agree and was often humiliated. Recently, they colluded with hoodlums and impersonated detectives, forcing me to sign a contract to sell the business, but I refused. I originally planned to file a lawsuit in court, but I have no money. After thinking about it, I could not bear the oppression, so I jumped into the river, etc. A yellow paper grievance and an account book were found on Sun. The district chief, considering that Sun's confession was pitiful, ordered him to be escorted to the General Public Security Bureau for interrogation in the afternoon.

Trial of the Wrongful Death of Wang Xiaomei 172

▲Debate Concluded Yesterday, Awaiting Sentencing

Zhang Tianxing, the leader of the third team of the Self-Defense Corps in Delan Lane No. 22, Shipi Lane, shot and killed his fiancée Wang Xiaomei with a pistol on the 8th of this month. Prosecutor Li completed the investigation of this case and believed that although Zhang Tianxing had no intention to kill, the responsibility for causing death through negligence could not be waived. Therefore, he filed a public prosecution citing Article 291 of the Criminal Law. The trial was held by Judge Deng yesterday morning. The defendant Zhang Tianxing stated that Wang Xiaomei herself pulled the gun to look at it, causing a stray bullet to be fired and killed. The official asked, "She used her hand to pull it, you should have stopped her." (Answer) "I didn't expect it." (Question) "There were bullets in the gun, you shouldn't have let her pull it." (Answer) "She came up from downstairs and immediately started pulling it." (Question) "Did you have a grudge against Wang Xiaomei?" (Answer) "No." (Question) "Did you deliberately kill her?" (Answer) "If I wanted to kill her, I wouldn't have scheduled a wedding date with her." (Question) "Who are Wang Xiaomei's family members?" (Answer) "Her parents and brother." At this point, his brother Zhang Jinfu testified, "Wang Xiaomei was shot on the 8th of this month. Although I was in the room, I didn't see how it happened." A neighbor, Xu Zhongyuan, testified that he lived at number 21, and he only heard about it afterwards, saying that she was playing with a handgun, which resulted in her death. He did not witness it. At this point, Prosecutor Li made his closing statement, mainly arguing that the defendant could not waive his criminal responsibility and requested that he be sentenced according to law. The defendant's defense lawyer, Sha Xunyi, requested that the defendant be declared innocent or, if found guilty, that the sentence be suspended. The judge announced the conclusion of the debate, scheduled the sentencing date, and adjourned the court.

▲Li Zhongyi Admits to Lending Money at Exorbitant Interest Rates

A local man named Chen, residing at number 49 Zhao Jiawan outside Xiaonanmen, works in a foreign company, so his family has considerable savings, which has made him a target for bandits. Unexpectedly, they received another letter the other day, in which the wording was very intense, and they were asked to bring the money to the wood in front of the Zhengde Elementary School in Huang Xinyi Ham between 9:00 PM and 10:00 PM. Use old newspapers as a sign. Chen immediately reported to the South Station Seventh Detachment of the Songhu Self-Defense Corps for investigation.

Upon hearing the report, team leader Ma Wenda, went to Pudong for entertainment that night. The team members Gu Guoan, Zhang Rengui, Jin Shunchang, Zhang Sheng, Yu Ruixiang, Peng Rongzhu, etc. went in disguise. They did not go with the director of the third sub-office of the first district in charge of the area. After arriving at the destination, they saw a newspaper on the wood. Each lurked in the bamboo fence on the other side. At about 11:00 PM, a tall person came to take the newspaper. The team members rushed forward and ordered him to stop. At that time, the man still moved forward. Team member Gu Guoan immediately drew a pistol and fired at him, hitting him in the right armpit. He was injured and bleeding on the spot, and was immediately arrested and sent to the first district and third sub-office to ask for instructions. The director of the sub-office Jin ordered them to return to the team and prepare a formal document for verification, because he had not been notified of the matter in advance. The team members sent the injured person to Shanghai Hospital for treatment, and notified team leader Ma to return to the team by phone. The injured person was sent to Shanghai Hospital for treatment. It is said that the man's name is Li Zhongyi, 37 years old, from Zhili, and he has been living with his wife Wang in house number 37 Tangfang Lane outside Xiaonanmen for many years. They have three sons. The eldest is named A Xing, who is 17 years old, the second is named Didi, who is also three years old, and the youngest is only three months old and is still in swaddling clothes. I usually lend money at high interest rates for a living. Last night I went to Chouchang Street to collect high-interest money. When I passed Huang Xinyi Ham, I suddenly saw a newspaper on the wood. Because the copper coins I was carrying were too heavy, I went forward to pick up the newspaper, intending to wrap the copper coins. Suddenly, many people came up and grabbed me. Because they were afraid that I would resist, they fired a shot and hit me in my right armpit. The bullet did not penetrate. Now the doctor has managed to remove the bullet. It is said that the injury is not serious, but after the wound heals, my right hand may be disabled.

Henan Province Relief Association Petitions for Relief Funds 177

▲ The Current Situation is Extremely Urgent

To Chairman Xu and Committee Member Wang of the Shanghai Office of the Relief Committee of Yunnan Road, Shanghai: The urgency for disaster relief in Henan has been repeatedly telegraphed. Currently, the counties of Luoyang, Zhengzhou, Bianliang, and Qinbo Mengxin have taken in 100,000 disaster victims, but the relief funds have been exhausted. There is no sustenance for raising them, and no funds for sending them away. The precarious situation is such that they do not even consider the next day. Looking around the disaster areas in various counties, many are unable to escape far due to transportation obstructions. The number of those who are displaced and dying is countless. The early autumn planting season is approaching, and food supplies are cut off. There are no seeds, and if cultivation is delayed, there will be another autumn famine. What have the people of Henan done to deserve this? They are facing imminent death. Our association lacks the resources to raise funds and is deeply worried. We have heard that American relief funds will be remitted to China. We earnestly request you to consider the severity of the disaster in Henan and allocate more funds for relief, providing prompt assistance to rescue the dying victims who are eagerly awaiting help. This telegram is urgent. We await your instructions. Zhang Fang, Relief Association of Henan Province, bows in supplication. The current situation is extremely urgent. The early autumn planting season is approaching, and the disaster areas have no farming tools or seeds. If cultivation is delayed, there will be another autumn famine. Disasters follow one after another, and there seems to be no end in sight. Unfortunately, Henan Province has once again fallen into the war zone. Transportation is obstructed, and life is cut off. Shanxi, Luoyang, Bianliang, Zhengzhou, Qinbo Mengxin have taken in nearly 100,000 disaster victims, providing food based on headcount. If the American funds can arrive early, please allocate them immediately. We earnestly request you to show compassion to the disaster victims and immediately allocate large sums of money to Henan, which will be managed by our association. We will prudently distribute funds and seeds to help them return to their hometowns. For those who are inherently poor and unemployed, we also request you to instruct the Pinghan and Longhai Railway Bureaus to order the stationmasters of each section to allocate vehicles to facilitate the transfer to the eastern provinces, allowing them to seek a livelihood on their own. We express these urgent words and hope you will pay attention. Zhang Fang, Relief Association of Henan Province, bows in supplication.

Central Bank Inspection Report 180

▲ 51st Time

The Supervisory Committee of the Central Bank, in accordance with Article 15 of the Central Bank Regulations, is responsible for inspecting the reserve funds for the Bank's issuance of convertible notes. The 51st inspection was held on April 19, 1920, at the Bank's Issuing Bureau. The results of the inspection are announced as follows: The total amount of convertible notes issued is 14,770,412 silver dollars, including 13,580,169 silver dollar notes and 1,190,243 auxiliary currency notes. The total amount of convertible note reserve funds is 14,770,412 silver dollars, including 9,847,407.2 silver dollars in cash reserve. The current cash reserve includes 6,196,128.31 silver dollars stored in the Bank's issuing vault, 1,138,135.14 silver dollars stored in branch banks in various ports, and 2,513,143.75 silver dollars deposited with other banks. The guaranteed reserve is equivalent to 4,923,004.8 silver dollars. According to Article 2 of the Central Bank Convertible Note Regulations, the cash reserve is 60% and the guaranteed reserve is 40%. This inspection found that the cash exceeded the 60% requirement, while the guaranteed reserve fell short of the 40% requirement, which is in accordance with the regulations. This report is hereby made. April 19, 1920, Supervisory Committee of the Central Bank, Chairman Li Fuxun, Supervisors Wu Jingli, Bei Songsheng, Qin Runqing, Yu Wangqing, Lin Kanghou, Xu Jilu.

British Gunboat Runs Aground in Sichuan River 181

▲ Two British Consuls Safely Arrive in Chongqing

The North China Daily News reports that the British gunboat Peterel, en route from Yichang to Chongqing on April 17, carrying the British Consul-General in Chongqing, Deri, and the newly appointed Consul in Chengdu, Dulles, ran aground suddenly at noon on Sunday, 320 kilometers upstream from Changshou, after striking a reef. After a hasty inspection, it was immediately grounded on the left bank of the Yangtze River. The two consuls transferred to the Yichang of the Jiangjiang Company and proceeded to Chongqing, arriving safely at the port that night.

News of Japanese Ship Kamitsukimaru Running Aground 182

▲ Crew Members Rescued and Transported to Xiamen

The Wenhui News reports that the Japanese ship Kamitsukimaru ran aground on the Xiaozhou Reef near Limen Island, about 30 miles from Shantou, and was completely lost. According to the wireless message received by the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company from the Guangli, it is currently rescuing the crew of the wrecked Japanese ship. However, due to the dense fog at sea, the work is very difficult. The loss of the Japanese ship was also caused by the fog. The Guangli happened to be coming to Shanghai from Hong Kong and, after receiving the Japanese ship's wireless distress signal, ventured to rescue. According to subsequent telegrams, the Japanese crew members have now been transported to Xiamen by the Guangli.
