Free Talk

A Laughing Matter 187

— Seafarer

▲ Old Gentleman: This morning, a poor young man came to my door begging for food. I asked him to take my business card and go to your restaurant for a meal, which I will pay for. How much did he eat?

Restaurant Owner: A table of dishes costing three dollars, four catties of Shaoxing Huadiao wine, and ten cigarettes. I have already put it on your tab.

▲ Son: Father, didn't you teach me that I should never scold or beat anyone younger than me? Father: Yes, it's wrong to bully the small.

Son: Then please write a letter to the dormitory master at our school and teach him a lesson.

▲ A: If there is a beautiful woman who allows you to kiss her left cheek or her right cheek, which one would you choose?

B: I don't want the left or the right. I only want the one in between.

▲ A: You really look just like your father. You have his eyes, his nose, and his mouth.

B: And that's not all. I also have his old short shirt and old pants.

Dr. Margouliès' Anecdotes 188

— Qifei

Dr. George Margouliès, recently appointed by the French Ministry of Education, came to China to investigate higher education. He is very knowledgeable in Chinese studies, so after arriving in Beijing, he has been giving lectures and attending social events every day. Many of the people in the new capital are old friends of the doctor, and the doctor also likes Chinese students very much and goes to talk with them. He has the demeanor of Kong Rong. As for the doctor's past experiences and his lectures, various newspapers have already reported them. I will collect more of his anecdotes and record them in Free Talk. (The following is what the doctor said)

I love to recite Han Fu and Six Dynasties literature. Although I have translated them myself, I have always thought it was wrong. Han Fu and parallel prose each have their own beauty, and translation destroys their color and texture. It is like a flower, only the branches and trunk remain.

Chinese literature is unique and stands in opposition to the group of Western countries. It has its own essence, and neither can surpass the other. Common people compare Li Bai with Du Fu, which loses their unity and is meaningless.

I am deeply fascinated by China. If someone asks me to criticize it, I really don't know what to say. I have been immersed in Chinese culture for a long time, and this trip will fulfill my long-cherished wish.

Among Chinese poets, I love Tao Yuanming the most. He has a great influence on literary history, and the Tang and Song poets were all influenced by him. He took nature as his model and Lao Zhuang as his backbone, transforming the ornate into the simple and elegant. Tao is truly a poet of the world.

Chinese prose is very high in its realm and is indeed a specialized art. Its completion should be after the Tang and Song dynasties. I love its poetic meaning and mixed rhyme, such as Liu Zongyuan's travel notes. The Tongcheng school of the Qing dynasty is gentle and secluded, and I also like it.

The author used Mr. Zhao Shourun to make it easier for the doctor to listen to his voice. The first three sections of this article are what the doctor said at the time, and the latter two were heard by student Fang Weide. The doctor speaks Chinese when talking to people, using simple and straightforward language, mixed with colloquialisms. His erudition and talent are truly extraordinary.

A Short Record of Seeking Fragrance Under the Moon 189

— Jingmengdie

The weeping crabapple, also known as the Drunken Beauty, see Hui Feng's Ci Hua saying "This flower is only found in my hometown (Lingui). Grafted onto cherry trees. It has not been seen in northern Ji or southern Jiangnan." Now there are several of these flowers in the Wuxi Park. In the late spring of March, the flowering season is already over, but Mr. Qian Mingshan of Changzhou suddenly passed through Wuxi on business. In the evening, I served him drinks in the hotel, which is the park hotel. During the meal, Mr. Qian said that he had taken a walk in the park and saw that all the flowers had withered, but only a few crabapple trees were still smiling. It was very pleasant. He praised it endlessly. I then responded by saying, "Tonight, the moon shines on the crabapple blossoms. There is no need to burn red candles. Why not go again to seek fragrance under the moon and enjoy the remaining fun? Moreover, after several nights of wind and rain, the moon tonight is clearly intended by Chang'e to welcome honored guests. How can we carelessly disappoint her?" Mr. Qian smiled and nodded. After the meal, he and the other guests went downstairs and entered the park, winding their way to the crabapple blossoms. At that time, the crescent moon had just emerged from the clouds. Although the tall pines were shady, the light leaked through the gaps. The crabapple blossoms that first caught the moonlight suddenly appeared in color, like pearl light and precious energy, breaking through the darkness. However, the blush and halo of the Drunken Beauty were no longer recognizable. Only a white one like a pear blossom was seen. That lovely red child suddenly transformed into Wenjun in plain clothes and Guoguo with a bare face. It was strange. After a while, a layer of pale moonlight permeated the forest, blurring the outside of the flowers, like a veil or a crystal curtain, making people imagine the ancient walking screen ladies and the veiled palace maids. This is what one can gain under the moon. Its interest is very different from that of the whip silk hat shadow. Later, we left.

The Invention of Artificial Blood 190

— Guoxin

A Parisian dispatch reports that Mr. Naumoff, who has long served in the French army, recently invented a type of artificial blood. Its function is no different from that of human blood. It has been repeatedly tested by the most famous biologists in France, and they are all very satisfied. It is especially effective in treating blood loss.

When it was first invented, dogs were used as test subjects. The French first extracted all the blood from the dog's body, causing it to be on the verge of death. Then, this artificial blood was injected. In less than five minutes, the dog was jumping, eating, and drinking as usual.

Later, when the European War began, Naumoff applied this artificial blood to injured soldiers who had lost too much blood, and it was immediately effective. It is estimated that no fewer than several hundred people were saved.

The formula for its ingredients is very simple. The raw materials used are only soda salt and magnesium oxide powder. The reason for using magnesium oxide powder is that soda salt is very toxic and it is not enough to detoxify it.

According to Western medicine, the only treatment for blood loss is blood transfusion. However, it is not always easy to find a suitable donor. Now that this alternative has been invented, those suffering from blood loss can sleep soundly without worry.

A Record of Orchids Below the Wild Boar Peak of Ma'anshan 191

— Diweng

In the first ten days of the month, the rain had just cleared, and the spring was bright and clear. Two or three friends made an appointment to visit Ma'anshan in Kuncheng. Ma'anshan is named after its shape. The mountain produces strange stones that are as bright and clean as jade, so it is also called Yushan or Yu Peak. The eastern peak of the mountain has towering rocks stacked on top of each other, which is quite spectacular. At its foot is the tomb of Liu Longzhou. However, it is not as good as the western peak. The western peak is higher, and the rocks are constantly towering, looking like a group of beasts, so it is called Wild Boar Peak. On this day, we climbed from the eastern peak to the western peak. The fragrance of orchids wafted in, and we thought it must be the orchids planted by the monks in the Buddhist temple. When we arrived at the temple, there were no orchids. We asked the monks, and they replied that the orchids were below Wild Boar Peak, in the concave part of the valley. The flowers and leaves cannot be seen, but the fragrance of orchids can be smelled. This happens every year. Because the valley is secluded and deep, people dare not descend the dangerous cliff, so no one can transplant them. I sighed and said, "The orchid grows in an empty valley, and it does not stop being fragrant because it is not worn by anyone. This is what it means." A guest said, "Zheng Banqiao's poem has the line 'Discussing carrying poles on the street corner.' Why is it so cheap? And the inscription on the broken pot of orchids that he painted says, 'Now that I think about it carefully, there are no confidants. I broke the bird pot and went into the mountains again.' It is also fortunate." I said, "If I had known today, I would have regretted not doing it sooner. The orchids of this mountain are hidden in a secluded valley, touching people with their fragrance, and are not played with by people. It can be said that they have found their place." Afterwards, we went down from another path and sat on the grass in the sports field, looking at Wild Boar Peak. The orchids were even more amazing, and the fragrance of the orchids still lingered in our noses.

Aerial Eye 192

— Guoxin

American Mr. Francis Jenkins recently invented an aerial image transmitter. Whenever an aircraft passes in the air, images can be immediately transmitted everywhere by this image transmitter, so that those below can see the space they have traveled through without lifting a foot. Mr. Jenkins has now configured this instrument and will conduct a field test soon. He has named it the "Aerial Eye." This invention is not only for entertainment, but will also occupy an extremely important position in the military. During wartime, it can be used to observe the contents of the enemy's army using this aerial eye.

Travels in Nanyang (Sixteen) 193

— Linghua

On the 22nd, I visited Mr. Bao Chuanxian, the manager of the Commercial Press. The Commercial Press has made significant contributions to culture in Nanyang. They published my books fifteen years ago. We had a long conversation about cultural endeavors in Nanyang. Generally, the reason our overseas Chinese go abroad is nothing more than the immigration issue. It is said that Yunnan has a very good climate and terrain, and some people want to start new living communities there. However, other friends say that there is still much land in the Malay Peninsula that can be developed. In the future, there will be a continuous stream of Chinese people going abroad, and many may go to Malaya. There is a Mr. Wu Juefei who lives in Wuzhou, and he mentioned matters in Guangxi. I said, Guangxi has vast land and a sparse population, and its scenery is unparalleled. Some people in its political circles once wanted to immigrate one million people from the northern provinces. I initially thought it was unbelievable, but after touring Guangxi again a year later, I realized that there was a lot of wasteland, and it could accommodate more than one million immigrants. If the internal strife is quelled, Guangxi could be a good place to establish new villages, and obtaining land from the government would not require money. Mr. Bao asked me about regions in the north suitable for immigration. I said that the three northeastern provinces have very large areas, and many people from Shandong Province go there, but few from Jiangnan. Some people from Shandong also operate in the Suiyuan and Hetao areas, and I heard that Mr. Wang Hongyi has made good profits buying land and running reclamation there. However, for people from Jiangnan, the climate is ultimately too cold. The best place I know of is Guangxi. The Malayan issue is worth studying in the future. It could be a major outlet for us Chinese.

Although this place is overseas, there are plenty of poets and writers to see. There is a Tan Xie Poetry Society. I traveled around the hills with them. The most abundant thing here is coconut trees. In English, it's Cocoa or Coconut. The fruit is called a coconut, and they are everywhere, like willows in the north. They can be six or seven zhang, up to eight or nine zhang tall. They grow about one zhang or seven or eight chi each year. Their leaves droop and hang down, like hanging hair. The fruit is like a small watermelon, and the shell is very hard. It must be chopped with an axe. The meat of this large fruit is very edible and tastes like peanuts. The spring juice can be drunk. Each fruit contains one pound to at least half a catty of juice. The fruit can be made into oil, like peanut oil in our country, which can be eaten and used. It can also be made into sugar, but we people are not used to eating it. The juice can be made into curry, so the people of Nanyang call the coconut a divine tree. However, the trunk is herbaceous rather than woody. The stem stands straight up in the sky. Coconut groves are everywhere here, a place for scholars and ladies to rest. Poetic sentiments and lyrics are all related to the coconut grove. Therefore, I wrote a poem to commemorate it:

The coconut tree stands tall, several zhang high,

Its beautiful tresses are scattered by the wind.

The fruit can be eaten, the juice can be drunk,

Beneath the trees, the moonlight whispers.

Here, it is necessary to distinguish between the coconut tree and the betel palm. I asked people for a long time, and many gave vague answers. Later, I learned the distinguishing points. The betel palm is straight and thin, with small leaves. The leaves are at the tip. Coconut leaves are wide and numerous. The trunk is rough and not smooth. The beauty of the leaves of the Go tree are arranged at natural angles, just like a Chinese paper fan, which is also a wonder. There are also red lotus flowers, which are not flowers, but leaves that are made into flowers. They are everywhere and do not fall in all seasons, like hydrangea.

Wonderful Rat Poison 194

— Sang Junfu

A rat infestation is a great source of hatred in a home. They rummage around at night, disturbing people's peaceful sleep, destroying clothing, and causing plague. Their crimes are especially hateful and punishable. My friend Mr. Lu is close friends with the famous Shanghai doctor Hong Weitang. Yesterday, he came to my residence for a pleasant chat and described to me a wonderful rat poison recently invented by Doctor Hong. It was very interesting. He said that he had tried it in practice and it was very effective. It is truly effective. It can catch rats with almost no misses. Calling it a wonderful rat poison is no exaggeration. Therefore, I am recording his method and sending it to Juanweng, so that those who hate rats can know how to catch and kill them and live in peace.

The method is to grind "noisy willow catkins" into powder and mix it with "crab roe" to make a slurry. (Note: "Noisy willow catkins" and crab roe are sold in pharmacies everywhere.) Then, on benzoin, wait until it is dry, and insert the incense into a bowl of rice. At night, when it is quiet, light the incense. When the rats smell the fragrance, they will all flock to it. After about an hour, the rats will be severely stimulated by the poison and will be exhausted and unable to support themselves. They will collapse. Then we can easily catch them one by one, or feed them to a healthy cat, which will devour them completely. This method is excellent. However, one thing to pay attention to at the time is that the doors and windows of the room must be tightly closed, so that it is airtight, so that the fragrance does not leak out, and the effect will be magical. The method is simple. Homeowners, why not give it a try?

Dog's Memory 195

— Jia

Lu Liangsheng of She County was a merchant in Xuancheng. He raised a dog that accompanied him in and out for many years. A hunter admired its speed and agility and earnestly asked Lu to sell it to him, offering eight taels of silver. He took it back to Huizhou. Every time he went hunting, the dog's catch was twice that of other dogs. After three months, the dog suddenly disappeared. The hunter suspected that it had escaped back and searched for it to Lu's house. The dog was indeed there. When it saw the hunter, it quickly fled into the inner room and hid under the stove. No matter how he called it, it would not come out, as if it missed its old master and could not bear to leave. Liangsheng pitied it and returned the original price and kept the dog. From Huizhou to Xuancheng is more than 300 li away, and it was able to recognize its old road and return to its original owner. This further confirms the story of the yellow dog delivering letters, which is no lie. My friend was an official in Xuan and told me about it upon his return, so I wrote it down.

Warmth in the Heart (177) 196

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter Ten: Red Flames Rise to the Sky, Courtesan Admires Filial Piety, Red Carpet Laid Out, Famous Actors Met

At this time, Lord Yan whispered to Wen Guizhi, "After you finish your performance today, come to my lodging. I have something to say to you. Come by yourself. I won't send anyone to call you again." After listening to his words, Wen Guizhi went to Lord Yan's lodging after finishing her performance. Originally, they had a good relationship. That day, she stayed there. The next morning, Lord Yan gave her five hundred yuan and said, "Take this. The weather is getting warmer. Make the clothes you urgently need first. If it's not enough, ask me for more." Fortunately, it's been less than a month. In the future, you can make whatever clothes you like. I'll be going to Beijing after the festival. There are some things you can prepare." Originally, that night, Lord Yan had decided to marry Wen Guizhi. The two had discussed it thoroughly. However, according to the rules in Shanghai's brothels, there are all sorts of troubles when marrying in the middle of a season. Therefore, they procrastinated for more than ten days, waiting for the Dragon Boat Festival to pass. Then Wen Guizhi removed her sign and officially became a respectable woman. She followed Lord Yan away. That Lord Yan was a famous scholar. Wen Guizhi jumped from a 'mo er' to a 'chang san,' and she was also a beauty. A famous scholar and a beauty naturally make a great match. As the ancients said, "May all lovers be united." Lord Yan and Wen Guizhi were not quite lovers, but later, it was said that they could not grow old together. Wen Guizhi still left. What was the reason for this? In the first few years, it was still good. Wen Guizhi had a younger sister named Wen Guifang. Lord Yan even acted as a matchmaker and sent her to a noble in Beijing. Later, Wen Guizhi gradually felt unaccustomed to living there. She also felt that Lord Yan's temper was difficult to handle. Originally, there are rules in official residences, especially in the homes of officials. People from brothels are not used to being restrained in that way. Lord Yan was a famous scholar, and once he became an official, he had a kind of unspoken temper. When she felt uncomfortable in her heart, she felt uncomfortable everywhere. At that time, there was only one way to separate. So, in the past, there was a certain famous scholar who married a famous actress. It was good at first, but later it gradually became unbearable. The famous scholar had an analogy, although it was to excuse himself, it was very appropriate. He said that all famous prostitutes and actresses are like a kingfisher with a beautiful voice and beautiful colors. It is best to let them sing, fight and fly freely in the forest. If you keep them in a cage, they will become listless and lifeless, and just die. Marrying a famous prostitute or actress as a concubine is like putting a kingfisher in a cage. At that time, there are only two ways. One way is to lock it to death in the cage. The other way is to open the cage and let the kingfisher fly freely into the forest.

Gold Market Weakens After Financial Opening 197

▲ The entire city only fluctuated by two taels. The gold exchange opened as usual yesterday. The bidding situation was mediocre. The front market only fluctuated by two taels, and the after-market only moved one tael in either direction, hovering around 98 taels. As for the contraction and expansion of foreign exchange, the market was not busy. Fuchang, Yuancheng Yong, and others bought, while Yuan Mao Yong and Xiangyu and others sold. From the morning, because the large silver bars stopped work internally, there was a slight setback. Later, buyers became active and raised the price, but the sellers were also diligent. Bills of exchange tended to be loose and once weakened, but then the banks repeatedly absorbed spot goods, causing them to be pulled up. At noon, it was between 99 taels. In the after-market, Wanxing and Yuancheng Yong advanced slightly, Zhifeng Yong and retail investors sold, and the market atmosphere became more mediocre, and the price also weakened slightly.

▲ The opening price fell by six qian. The recent unified core of British silver bars increased by 1/16, the far-term increased by 1/8, the silver price was reduced by 1/8, and the exchange rate did not change. The opening price for the June bid was 498 taels and 5 qian, a slight decrease of six qian. The gross price rose from 98 taels 3 qian to 9 taels 7 qian, because the buyers saw more. Bills of exchange were stable. The bank absorbed recent Japanese gold at 104.8125 and bought British gold at 11 pence 1875, and the posted prices remained unchanged. At that time, it returned to 9 taels 12 qian, and the sellers gradually increased. Bills tended to be thin. Mitsui bought far-term Japanese gold at 1 tael 0 fen 3.625, Datong sold recent British gold at 11 pence 1875, and the gold price was also weak, eventually falling to 97 taels 5 qian, followed by fluctuations of 45 qian. Silk and Tea Lake Districts' Silkworm Rearing Affected by Banditry 210

As the Grain Rain solar term arrives, farmers in the interior are engaged in hatching silkworm eggs. The old Huzhou prefecture has historically been a well-known silkworm silk region. This year, the lake bandits are rampant, looting everywhere. Farmers rearing silkworms along the lake have discarded the silkworm eggs they had reserved, warning each other not to raise them. Even the number of silkworm eggs hatched by silkworm farmers in Jili and other places has decreased. It is difficult to expect a bumper spring harvest in the Lake district this year.

Wuyuan Green Tea Harvested and Processed Early 212

Wuyuan Gao Zhuang green tea, which is most popular in the UK, US, Russia, and France, will soon be on the market. In the past month, tea firms have been preparing to open their businesses, and the atmosphere is very prosperous. However, due to the recent cold weather, the tea buds have been suppressed by the cold, and their growth has slowed down. The local tea industry association issued a notice yesterday, advising mountain farmers to harvest and process the tea early, so as to avoid old tea leaves becoming loose and being disliked by foreigners. However, mountain farmers complained that this year's grain prices have soared, with each dan of tea rice costing 15 yuan, coupled with rising labor and commodity prices. It is expected that future tea prices will not only be lower than in the past but may even have to be raised. Tea firms are facing financial difficulties, and the prices of firewood and charcoal have all risen, so the cost has increased rather than decreased. Therefore, although there are not fewer tea firms in various villages than in the past, the owners are deeply worried about this year's situation.

Fuliang Green Tea Will Be Available Soon 213

In addition to supplying foreign firms with tea leaves for making black tea, Fuliang also sells a considerable amount of green tea to local tea shops each year. This year, the tea trees in the area sprouted quite early due to the warm weather last month. Tea from Naxiang Zhouyuan will be available for harvesting within days. Tea shops in Jingzhen and Raozhou have recently sent personnel to Fuliang to search for purchases, and new tea will be available soon.

Qimen New Black Tea Has Opened the Scales 214

Since the 15th, mountain farmers in Qimen have mostly started picking new black tea. Fortunately, the weather has been sunny and the quality of the water is still good. The scales for Ling Shou's pre-rain Bai Hao have been opened, with each dan priced at 140 yuan, similar to last year. However, due to the recent rice shortage in Qimen and the fact that the tea-making workers were unable to come to Qimen for employment due to the Communist bandits attacking the Hekou area, it has been difficult to proceed quickly with harvesting and processing.

Morocco Tea News Not Good 215

French Morocco is the largest market for our country's green tea. The sales of Zhen Mei, Zhu Cha, Xiu Mei, and other varieties from Wuyuan, Tunxi, and other areas have increased from 30,000 to 40,000 boxes to more than 100,000 boxes in the past five or six years. Last year, due to the suspension of sales to Russia, foreign merchants took the opportunity to hoard goods. The import of Chinese tea into Morocco increased by 40,000 to 50,000 boxes compared to the previous year, resulting in full inventories and a sharp drop in tea prices. Many foreign tea merchants suffered losses. Shanghai traders have adopted a negative attitude towards this year's new tea due to the unfavorable news from that market.

Automobile News and Commentary

The 514 Feixia New Car: Yellow Shadow Stays... 222

▲ Countless Amazing Achievements

If we look back over the past ten years, every new car produced by the Feixia Factory has been welcomed by society. For this reason, the sales of various Feixia vehicles have grown rapidly in recent years. Since the new cars of previous years have achieved such excellent results, it can be asserted that the new car produced this year will certainly not have any shortcomings. Since the end of the Great War, the Feixia Car Factory has launched the 501 new car on the market. Following the 501, the 94-horsepower 509 new car was launched. Almost everyone in the world acknowledges this new car as an excellent product.

▲ Beautiful Body: Take the 514 Feixia new car as an example. The beauty of the body is unprecedented. Although the length of the wheelbase is not much different from that of the 94-horsepower Feixia car, the space inside the car is wider. Even if four people sit in it together, it is unusually comfortable and without the suffering of crowding. The strength of the horsepower is such that, although the UK and other countries have been increasing the tax rate in recent years, the economics of various Feixia new cars have long been evident. The engine of the new car produced this year is also quite large, measuring 143,800. Therefore, the ratio of weight makes people very eager to buy cars. To date, the number of owners who have purchased the 509 new car is countless. Now, the 514 new car is meeting us again. The new car this year is very different from the old car. The construction method is completely different. From the buffer rail to the taillights, the manufacturing process has been carefully studied to ensure that the produced vehicles satisfy modern car owners. Other things, such as the excellent raw materials and low value, are even more important. The advantages of the 514 Feixia new car are analyzed below, which I believe will also be welcomed by the readers of this publication.

The actual horsepower is 11.14, and the maximum can reach 34. It can rotate 3,400 revolutions per minute. There are four cylinders. The cast model is 674,102 CCMM in length. The bore and stroke, cylinders, and crankcase are all connected in one piece. The top is equipped with an excited head cover with 16 solid nails. The crankcase has three obvious and simple bearings to govern the movement of the crank rod. The crank rod has four bearings, which are used to imitate the Morse silent chain. This chain passes through the generator's rod to control the power. All the pistons are equipped with appropriate small dents on one side to act as guides. The water pump, which is installed in the front part of the cylinder, has a rod that comes out of the pulley on the crank rod to control the movement of the water pump. There is an iron fan with four blades on the handle of the water pump. The connecting rods are also connected to each other in one piece. The pistons are made of lead and have three compression rings. The upper part of the cylinder crankcase is also connected in one place. The oil drainer is also made of high-quality steel, so there is no obstruction during operation. There are no accidents when disassembling the piston and connecting rod. In terms of the overall construction method of the Feixia new car, the main bearings, as well as the camshaft bearings, connecting rods, iron chains, and other items, are connected to the crankcase by a gear-type water pump to govern the camshaft. The pressure is quite high, so the convenience of all lubrication is unmatched by any vehicle.

▲ Powerful Electricity: The electrical system is governed by generators, batteries, and coils. The distribution of current is very convenient, and the power generation is also relatively strong. The above-mentioned distributor is placed on top of the cylinder. The spark plugs are installed at an angle. The automatic generator is installed next to the engine, running in parallel. A ring-shaped gear is installed on the left side to block the flywheel. The carburetor is a Solex type, installed next to the piston. The mixture of air is supplied from the exhaust chamber to the intake pipe. In addition, there is a gasoline ejector to make driving more convenient. There is also a common throttle device on the carburetor to help air flow. The installation of the new car is so complete that the gasoline is poured into the oil tank and into the carburetor without any accidents. As for the installation of the oil tank, it can be divided into two parts, which are forged and connected to the flange. It passes through the metal dashboard, and the dashboard has 12 screws nailed into it. The installation and removal are easy. There are rubber materials mixed in to reduce vibration, and the installation of the oil tank also strengthens the dashboard. There is no major explosive force in any environment. Moreover, in the event of a special accident, it is quite convenient to remove it from the engine. A funnel is installed under the flame arrester. In addition, there is a advantage that I would like to tell the readers, that is, a V-shaped convex line is installed under the engine so that gasoline can travel in two channels without exploding. There is a plate under the carburetor. If a fire occurs while driving, this plate can be used to extinguish it in any environment. Therefore, no fire will occur no matter what.

▲ Engine Installation: The engine and chassis are joined in four main places. There are spherical rubbers installed in between to cushion. Two of them are near the engagement part, which is also the most important part of connecting the engine. The other two are in the front, crossing the frame. The simple engagement device is equipped with a circular handle, which is very dry during operation and does not require attention. The gearbox is made of aluminum and has four-part acceleration. It is also screwed to the engagement device. The same is true for other important places. The small gears full of mesh holes make the car run without any noise. In terms of the speed of each part, the speed is 50, 34 and 3/4, 21 and 3/4, 12 and 3/4 miles per hour. When going up or down hills, the slope can also reach one-third. The weight of the propeller shaft is uniform and unparalleled. The connecting head is used to take the power from the gearbox and feed it into the semi-floating rear axle. The ratio of the inclined gears from 5.6 to 1 is spiral. The axle housing is also uniquely designed, with two steel pressure devices running horizontally. The connection with the front is also screwed. The disassembly is convenient, and the hub caps are placed inside.

▲ Semi-Elliptical Springs: The springs installed in each part, regardless of front and rear, are semi-elliptical. As for the hooks and needles, they are all lubricated with the Tecalemit method. The diameter of the four-wheel brakes is quite wide and long, and the brake drums are also made of aluminum. The foot pedals and handrails can be used at will. This type of brake has even more amazing results, and the construction method is completely different from other vehicles. The small nails used are very suitable. There is a total screw nailed to the floor, and at the same time there are four-winged nails tied to the end of each connecting rod to control the brake cam handle. The engine is affected by the fan and heat. Driving on British roads is unprecedentedly stable, fast, and convenient. The foot pedals are of moderate length and can be placed on the left or right. The gear change and brake operation are all very easy. The switch for turning off the headlights is located in front of the driving system and has an electric switch. When starting the car, you only need to step on the foot pedal. The advantages are countless.

▲ Beautiful Appearance: The aluminum heat sink is tall and slightly narrow, which really enhances the beauty of the vehicle. As for its style, it is like a honeycomb, with only inclined iron pipes installed on it. The wheelbase of the 11.14-horsepower Feixia new car is 8 feet, 4 and 3/4 inches. The wheelbase is 4 feet. The length of the body is 6 feet, 6 inches, and the length of the chassis is 11 feet, 6 inches. The flat round wheels are completely made of steel, and the tires are 27 x 4.75. The construction of the body is even more unexpected. The four-door sedan has three lights on each side, and the two-door passenger car has two large windows. As for the factory cars and two-seater convertible sports cars, the seats are unusually comfortable. In a nutshell, the 11.14-horsepower new car is unmatched by any vehicle in terms of beautiful appearance and comfortable driving. It is truly worthy of being the most valuable six-cylinder product of the Feixia Company.

Historical Fragments of Rubber 223

Millions of car users are limited in their ability to understand the complexity of tire manufacturing and the difficulty of cultivating rubber trees, especially those who are far from the rubber-producing areas. Recently, Dunlop Rubber Company planted 2 million rubber trees in 16 square miles of land in the Malay Peninsula. It is expected that in ten years, it can reach 5,000 tons of rubber per year. The company currently has about 4 million grown rubber trees, producing 8,500 tons of rubber per year.

The procedure for extracting rubber in the producing area is very complicated. A container is placed under each rubber tree. Every other day, a thin layer of bark is cut to wait for the rubber tree sap to drip. The sap dripping from each tree in one day can only produce half an ounce of dry rubber.

One-third of the farmers who cultivate rubber trees are Chinese, and the rest are natives. The local rubber company built temples and houses for these farmers, established hospitals and schools, and supplied them with cheap rice.

Automobile Pilot

When a ship sails in an unfamiliar waterway, it must hire a so-called pilot to guide its course. Now, pilots have also emerged in the automotive industry, which is a rare coincidence.

In London, foreign tourists often regret the difficulty of driving during traffic jams. Therefore, there are automobile pilots. These people can take responsibility for driving or just point out how to proceed. The fee is five shillings every two hours, which is also a new business.

Translation Compilation

World Automobile News 226

▲ The Strange Tale of Using Wine Instead of Water In the Ibani region of France, water sources are scarce, but grapes are abundant. As a result, automobile owners often worry about the lack of cooling water. Some insightful individuals have taken a large quantity of grapes and made juice from them, using wine to replace water. They sell it to car owners, taking advantage of this opportunity to do business. Car owners have no choice but to buy it and add it to their dried-up radiators as a supply. The price of wine is about twenty cents a barrel, while water is even more expensive. The area has contracted water vendors who specialize in carrying spring water and selling it to various villages at high prices.

▲ Paris Forbids Hard Rubber Tires Public buses in Paris, the capital of France, are all equipped with hard rubber tires. Therefore, they shake houses and create loud noises when traveling through the city. As a result, the Paris Public Works Bureau has strictly banned them.

▲ Danish Drivers Must Be Insured All automobile and motorcycle drivers in Denmark must pay a certain insurance fee to protect pedestrians. Denmark is said to be the second country to have this type of insurance law after a life insurance provider.

▲ Siamese Car Sales Methods Selling cars in Siam (Thailand) is quite difficult. During the day, people are busy with farming, and at night they are absorbed in theater. The local General Motors branch lacks suitable times to connect with customers and suitable places to negotiate prices, resulting in sluggish sales. They have now improved their methods by using theatrical performances to attract business. They perform publicity for twelve hours every night, and the sales volume of Chevrolets has greatly increased. This type of promotion method can be called an innovation in the world of commerce, and General Motors' advertising can be said to cater most to the psychology of people everywhere.

▲ Newly Invented Automobiles Switzerland and the United States have recently invented a substitute for gasoline. The Swiss invention is derived from charcoal, mostly used for trucks. It is said to be seven times more economical than ordinary gasoline. The American invention is extracted from shale, producing oil of pure and thick quality, refined and durable. It is said to increase horsepower by four times compared to ordinary gasoline.

▲ Spirit of Self-Governance The people of Berlin, the capital of Germany, drive cars without the supervision of traffic police. Everyone has a spirit of self-governance. Anyone who violates the usual laws can be arrested and warned by others who witness it.

▲ Indian Labor Cheaper than Machine Power India has a large population and cheap labor. It only costs ten cents a day to hire someone to carry heavy objects. Although the use of trucks is also widespread, their purpose is for work and economy. It is now rare to hear of human labor being cheaper than machine power.

▲ Germany Facilitates Travelers Those who travel to Germany gather outside major cities upon arrival. There, guides lead them and drive them to visit various scenic spots. This is very safe and saves time. They also provide travelers with driving rules at any time. Hiring such personnel costs little.

▲ Colombo Emphasizes Roadside Scenery According to Colombo's recent plan to reform roadside scenery, it is planned to remove all billboards and other similar posters along the way to beautify the roads and scenery. Government notices and road signs are of course not included in this plan.

▲ Australia Issues Parking Permits According to the parking regulations of Melbourne, all vehicles parked on the roadside must have a parking permit. The price of the permit is twenty-five cents. Before parking, the permit must first be shown to a police officer for inspection. Each permit is valid for the day and expires the next day.

▲ Chinese Exploration Team Uses Automobiles Instead of Camels Automobiles are used extensively, reaching far and wide, unafraid of rain or drought, or ice and snow. They can handle any weight. The Sino-French exploration team organized by China and France in North China and Annam originally planned to use camels to carry all the luggage, but now they are using automobiles instead. The Chinese explorers departed from Peiping (Beijing) last month and are heading to Russian Turkestan, where they will meet with Persian and French explorers.

Records

The Danger Level of Automobiles… Honk… 227

Every day we read newspapers, and records of pedestrians being killed by cars are almost too numerous to count. Moreover, as the number of cars increases daily, the number of accidents also increases endlessly. But to only focus on the increase in accidents without considering the number of cars and the volume of traffic is hardly fair to simply condemn cars as dangerous elements.

According to statistics from the British Automobile Association, the number of registered cars in the UK in 1928 was 2,019,167. In that year, the number of car accidents was 111,976, with an index of 55 per thousand. Tracing back to 1918, this index was 81 per thousand, and in 1919 it was 101 per thousand. In the five years leading up to the present, the annual accident index has been approximately 50 to 55 per thousand.

Judging from these numbers, even without considering the annual increase in the number of cars, it can be seen that the number of accidents has decreased rather than increased.

Furthermore, considering the statistics of automobile traffic volume, in a certain location at the same time, the number of cars passing through in 1929 was five times more than in 1923. However, the number of cars only increased threefold in these six years. In other words, if each car traveled 7,000 miles per year six years ago, it now travels 12,000 miles. This means that not only is the number of cars increasing year by year, but the distance they travel is also increasing year by year. With a large number of cars and busy traffic, the chance of accidents is actually easier than several years ago. According to the above statistics, only a decrease in the accident index is seen. From this, it can be proved that the danger level of cars has been decreasing almost every year.
